# CLAUDE.md

Canonical project context for VihuStudio. Read this first before making any change.

## Product Vision

- Preserve what is real.
- Beautify originals rather than replacing them.
- VihuStudio is a non-destructive visual storytelling studio.

## Core Principles

- Visual controls for visual properties.
- Text controls for textual properties.
- Reusable components over one-off implementations.
- Editor UI should only contain controls that improve the active workflow.
- Metadata should not occupy permanent workspace.
- Architecture changes require explicit approval.
- Repository is the source of truth.

## Current Status

### Frozen (Version 1.0)

- Workspace
- Project Management
- Persistence
- Page Management (Sprint 8.2 drag-and-drop reorder + trimmed context menu)
- Theme Engine (Sprint 9.2 ŌĆö sits atop `ThemeRegistry`, not a hardcoded array; every public method keeps its pre-9.2 signature; Sprint 9.3 adds `getActiveArtworkTheme(Id)` / `applyArtworkTheme` alongside, same signature-preservation discipline)
- Theme Registry / Theme Library (Sprint 9.2 ŌĆö Theme Library Foundation: `js/themeRegistry.js` merges Official + Imported themes into one catalog behind `get(id) / list() / getCatalog()`; `.vtheme` package format ŌĆö plain JSON, `{manifest, theme, assets}` ŌĆö validated on import with friendly failures, never crashes; duplicate-id imports prompt Replace / Keep Both / Cancel; imported themes persist to `localStorage`, official themes ship with the app; architecture is additive-ready for Theme Creator / Theme Editor / Theme Export / Community Themes without another redesign ŌĆö none of those ship in 9.2)
- Artwork Themes (Sprint 9.3 ŌĆö second theme type on the same registry, `manifest.type: 'story'|'artwork'`, missing/invalid `type` normalizes to `'story'` so every pre-9.3 package keeps loading with zero migration; controls ONLY how a child's picture is presented ŌĆö background / frame / paper / caption / shadow / lighting / composition ŌĆö NEVER touches artwork pixels; layered into the existing Sprint 6.5/6.5.1 Picture Border system as one more `_resolveBorder` fallback layer, not a parallel rendering engine; opt-in, no default, a "None" tile clears it; five Official Artwork Themes ŌĆö Museum Gallery ┬Ę Sketchbook ┬Ę Watercolor Portfolio ┬Ę Classroom Display ┬Ę Scrapbook; Theme Library shows Story Themes / Artwork Themes as two sections in the same modal)
- Dynamic Theme Workspace (Sprint 9.4 ŌĆö an optional `theme.editor` block, resolved by the new `js/workspaceBuilder.js`, decides which presentational controls the right-side designer shows, in what order, per theme; editor-only ŌĆö never touches rendering. Single active-workspace-theme rule, no merging: an active Artwork Theme's `editor` governs Slide/Frame/Holder if present, otherwise the Story Theme's does. Slide = Page Designer's Story tab (Decorations, theme-gated; Background/Title stay core, always shown); Frame = Card Designer's Frame Look + Frame Style groups inside the Picture section (`frameStyle`/`fill`/`border`/`radius`/`shadow`, plus new `paper`/`mat`); Holder = Card Designer's Picture/Text/Sticker sections' presentation controls (`presentation`/`artworkFrame`/`lighting`/`caption` for Image, `typography`/`alignment` for Text, `stickerShadow` for Sticker ŌĆö all additive to the always-present manipulation controls). Five official themes ship an `editor` block (Storybook Classic, Comic, Museum Gallery, Sketchbook, Watercolor Portfolio); Adventure/Minimal/Classroom Display/Scrapbook have none and fall back to today's fixed control set unchanged ŌĆö the real backward-compatibility proof)
- Theme Language v2 (Sprint 9.5 ŌĆö new `js/themePresets.js` registry adds a Presentation Preset layer that resolves Presentation Preset ŌåÆ Theme Overrides ŌåÆ System Defaults, so a theme can name creative intent (`presentation:'gallery'`) instead of spelling out every low-level field; does not redesign Theme Registry / Theme Engine / Workspace Builder. A Story Theme opts in with an optional `slide` block (page-furniture defaults ŌĆö panelStyle/footerStyle/pageNumber/bookTitle*/handle*/decorations, read by `ThemeEngine._defaultOptionsFor`) and/or an optional `holder` block (Picture Holder look defaults ŌĆö cornerRadius/padding/shadow/fill, the sprint's "Frame" scope; named `holder` to match the existing `themeOptions.holder` schema and avoid colliding with the pre-existing `theme.frame` field, which is the book's outer frame COLOR, an unrelated concept). An Artwork Theme's existing `presentation` field (Sprint 9.3) now resolves through `HOLDER_PRESETS.image` in `renderer/slideRenderer.js`'s `_artworkBorder`. `js/workspaceBuilder.js`'s Presentation control sources its options from `ThemePresets.listHolderPresets` instead of a hardcoded list, and a theme with a `presentation` but no `editor` block gets a non-empty control list from that preset's `editorControls` metadata. Storybook Classic's `slide`/`holder` presets reproduce its pre-9.5 hardcoded values exactly (byte-identical render verified) so the app's default theme has zero regression; Museum Gallery / Sketchbook / Watercolor Portfolio are refactored to the shorthand form, Comic gets richer `slide`/`holder` presets, Classroom Display / Scrapbook are untouched ŌĆö all backward compatible, no migration required)
- Museum Gallery Theme Support (Sprint 9.6 ŌĆö Phase 2, Official Theme Collection kickoff. Museum Gallery is the reference implementation; the engine only grew where this one theme needed it, nothing speculative. New capabilities, all additive: (1) **Folder-based `.vtheme` packages** ŌĆö `js/zipReader.js` (dependency-free ZIP reader, `DecompressionStream('deflate-raw')`) lets `ThemeEngine.importThemeFile` accept a real zipped package (manifest+theme `.vtheme`, `metadata.json`, `preview.png`/`thumbnail.png`, `layouts/` `frames/` `layer-packs/` `assets/`) alongside the untouched legacy flat-JSON path; `themes/MuseumGallery.vtheme` ships as a real importable package proving zero app-code changes are needed after import. (2) **Slide layout presets** ŌĆö `theme.layouts` (Portrait/Landscape/Square/Wide/Quote/Full Bleed) resolves the Frame rect via `renderer/slideRenderer.js`'s `_resolveLayout`/`_panelRectFor`, replacing the hardcoded PANEL_X/Y/W/H; `portrait` is byte-identical to the old fixed rect so every theme without `layouts` (everything but Museum Gallery) is unaffected. `holders:1` on every preset reserves ŌĆö but doesn't yet build ŌĆö multi-Holder layouts (Diptych/Triptych are a deliberate future sprint, not bolted on here). (3) **Frame Variations** ŌĆö `theme.frameVariations` (named artwork-field bundles: Classic White Mat, Warm Ivory, Natural Linen, Floating Frame, Black Matte, Gold Accent, Dark Gallery), chosen per-card and resolved as one more override layer on the Sprint 9.5 preset ladder; this is also where Sprint 9.4's per-card Holder controls (Presentation/Frame/Lighting/Caption/Paper/Mat), written since 9.4 but never rendered, finally activate. (4) **Holder "Original" mode** ŌĆö `ImageViewEngine`'s third mode alongside Fit/Fill (natural pixel size, zoom still applies on top); a universal core control (`_setMode` in `js/cardDesigner.js`), not theme-gated. (5) **The Layer System** ŌĆö `js/layerEngine.js`, a small generic engine (layer = `{type:text|sticker|decoration, target:slide|frame|holder|element, anchor, zIndex, visible, ...}`) with zero canvas code of its own (SlideRenderer supplies the draw primitives); Museum Gallery's 5-layer pack (Museum Caption, Page Number, Handle, Gallery Spotlight, Wax Seal) is the only consumer this sprint ŌĆö Page Number/Handle are declarative-only entries (no `text` payload) since they keep rendering via the pre-existing `_drawHandle`/`_drawPageNumber`, never duplicated. (6) **Rich theme metadata** ŌĆö optional manifest fields (`purpose`/`mood`/`bestFor`/`notRecommendedFor`/`themeIcon`/`previewImage`), shown in the Theme Library picker card when present; `ThemeRegistry.registerOfficial` copies them from an official theme's own object onto its auto-derived manifest. (7) **Global packs** ŌĆö Social + Shape sticker categories added to `js/stickerLibrary.js`'s existing extensible catalog (no architecture change), and `js/emojiPicker.js` wires an insert-emoji control onto every Text Element content field via `js/pageDesigner.js`'s shared `_makeTextInput`. Every change verified byte-identical-render-safe for themes that don't opt in)
- Museum Gallery Fidelity (Sprint 9.7 ŌĆö matched Museum Gallery against the approved Design Board; visual fidelity, not new functionality, extending the theme language only where the board demanded it. (1) **Frame Variations carry real values** ŌĆö `matWidth`/`frameThickness`/`borderColor`/`wallTone` on each variation (not just enum lookups); `frameThickness>0` finally enables the artwork border stroke (`lineEnabled` was hardcoded off for every artwork theme through 9.6); `wallTone` is the gallery-room paint colour, a Slide-level concept distinct from the mat, resolved independently of the image-gated Picture Border pipeline (`_resolveWallTone`) so it applies even on image-less pages (Quote). Base "Classic White" values live on `js/themePresets.js`'s `gallery` preset so the variation itself can stay an empty override. (2) **Layouts are compositions, not just rects** ŌĆö a layout preset's `composition` (`'below'` default, `'right'` for Wide, `'quote'` for Quote) decides where the Museum Caption sits and whether the Frame/Holder pipeline runs at all; Quote drops the Frame entirely for a centered, word-wrapped quote + attribution (`_drawQuoteText`), Wide moves the caption beside the Frame (`_captionRectFor`) instead of below it. (3) **Museum Caption composes real fields** ŌĆö `slide.metadata.artworkTitle/artist/age/date`, rendered as a two-line museum label (`_drawMuseumCaption`) via the Layer Engine's `museumCaption` text source; edited through a new `museumCaption` Workspace control (Title/Artist/Age/Date, each with emoji insertion). (4) **Handle/Page Number position + colour are theme-drivable** ŌĆö a Layer Pack entry's optional `position` field pins Handle/Page Number to a corner regardless of the Story Theme's own default (Museum Gallery: page number bottom-left, handle bottom-right, matching the board); a wall-tone luminance check (`_chromeTextColor`) keeps that text legible against both light and dark gallery walls without hardcoding one mood. Every change verified against a live render comparison with the board and byte-identical for themes that don't opt in)
- Theme Designer (Sprint 8.4.2 ŌĆö Book Style ┬Ę Branding ┬Ę Typography ┬Ę Colours ┬Ę Picture Holder Defaults ┬Ę Page Layout ┬Ę Decorations ┬Ę Navigation; sub-options ride on `themeOptions` and reach the renderer via `ThemeEngine.resolveTheme()`)
- Card Designer (Sprint 8.4.3 ŌĆö explicit Theme ŌåÆ Card inheritance: header note + per-section "Theme / This Page" badge; Picture Holder ┬Ę Picture ┬Ę Sticker ┬Ę Text ┬Ę Decoration sections ŌĆö every object follows the same Object Designer interaction model)
- Page Designer (­¤ō¢ Story / ­¤ōś Cover / ­¤¬Ø Hook / ­¤Åü End roles; per-role content editors; per-element checklist with Visibility / Lock / Reset)
- Sticker Studio (15 categories, search, favorites + recents, 241 stickers; insertions land in the Card Designer's Sticker section)
- Picture Studio (temporary preparation modal ŌĆö Crop / Rotate / Flip / Auto Enhance / Fit-Fill / Reset / Before-After; bake-on-Apply through the canonical SlideRenderer path)
- Publish Studio (Sprint 9.0 ŌĆö five-stage flow: ­¤ō¢ Read My Story ŌåÆ Ō£© Almost Ready ŌåÆ ­¤Ä» Choose Story Destination ŌåÆ ­¤ōĢ Publishing ŌåÆ ­¤Äē Celebration; destination-driven ŌĆö Story Book (Digital / Print-ready PDF via `js/pdfWriter.js`), Story Carousel (Instagram Portrait / Square PNGs; ZIP for multi-page via `js/zipWriter.js`), Story Reel (Coming Soon, plug-in-ready via `StoryDestinations.register()`); WYSIWYE holds byte-identically between the editor canvas and Carousel Portrait PNG)
- WYSIWYE Rendering (Sprint 9.0.2 + 9.1.2 ŌĆö `SlideRenderer.init(canvas, opts)` accepts `{dpr}`, defaults to `window.devicePixelRatio`; `#previewCanvas` is CSS-fluid so the display fills the preview column up to native 1080 CSS px; the editor and the published Carousel Portrait PNG are byte-identical for the same slide ŌĆö `SHA-256=86e6910993d29932`; `SlideRenderer.buildPayload` stamps the *resolved* theme so Theme Designer overrides reach every render surface; hit-testing reads canonical size via `SlideRenderer.getCanvasSize()`)
- Story Destinations Registry (Sprint 9.0.4 ŌĆö `StoryDestinations.list / find / findFormat / register / validate` ŌĆö future destinations plug in from outside `storyDestinations.js` without editing PublishStudio; documented interface contract in the module header)
- Theme Designer Global Behaviour (Sprint 9.1.3 ŌĆö Theme changes propagate to every page + every thumbnail + publish output immediately; NO object selection required; `_invalidateThumbnails` clears every slide's cache, `buildPayload` uses `resolveTheme()` so Typography / Colours overrides reach the renderer through the payload)
- Publishing Language (Sprint 9.1.4 ŌĆö Export terminology is removed from the editor UI entirely; `­¤ō¢ Publish` is the only publishing CTA; page context menu carries the six child-friendly actions: Publish This Page ┬Ę Duplicate Page ┬Ę Move Page Up ┬Ę Move Page Down ┬Ę Add Blank Page After ┬Ę Delete Page; `PublishStudio.open({slides:[oneSlide]})` accepts a single-page slice for the Publish This Page flow)
- Universal Object Consistency (Frame ┬Ę Sticker ┬Ę Decoration ┬Ę Text-Holder ┬Ę Background all share Select / Move / Resize / Rotate / Layer / Lock / Delete primitives via the `slide.metadata.elementOverrides` bag)
- Universal Object Selection (Sprint 8.4.1 ŌĆö any object click switches to the Card Designer, expands the matching section, and smoothly scrolls it into view; one `SCENE_TYPE_TO_SECTION` mapping covers every selectable element type)
- Picture Holder Completion (Sprint 8.4.4 ŌĆö Selection ┬Ę Free Move ┬Ę Free W/H Resize ┬Ę Rotation ┬Ę Layer ┬Ę Lock ┬Ę Delete on the holder; Border / Corner Radius / Shadow shared with the Picture section's Frame Look + Frame Style; the picture inside the holder remains independently editable ŌĆö Zoom / Move / Replace / Fit / Fill)
- Creation Experience V1 / Child First Studio (Sprint 10.0 ŌĆö a Studio UX layer only; Theme Engine / Theme Registry / Theme Builder / Theme Import / Theme Library / rendering / the SlideŌåÆFrameŌåÆHolderŌåÆElement containership are all untouched. New product model ŌĆö Creation Type ŌåÆ Theme ŌåÆ Representation ŌåÆ Editor ŌåÆ Context Editing ŌĆö sits in front of the existing editor: `js/creationFlow.js` is a full-screen, hardcoded 3-step wizard (Creation Type cards ŌåÆ compatible Theme cards ŌåÆ Representation cards) shown on every fresh boot (no saved session) via `js/app.js`'s session-bootstrap IIFE; restoring a saved session skips it entirely. Only Story (`storybook-classic`) and Artwork Showcase (`museum-gallery`) are real this sprint ŌĆö Quote Design / Poems show a "Coming Soon" card rather than a half-working editor. A Theme with Representations (Museum Gallery: ShowcaseŌåÆ`landscape`, PortraitŌåÆ`portrait`, QuoteŌåÆ`quote`, mapped to its existing `theme.layouts` ids) shows Step 3; a Theme with none (Storybook Classic) skips straight to the editor. Selecting a Representation only ever writes to fields the runtime already reads ŌĆö `slide.metadata.layout`, `AppState.project.artworkTheme`/`.theme` ŌĆö via `PageOps.addBefore(0)` + `ThemeEngine.applyArtworkTheme`/`applyTheme`, so nothing downstream needed to change. `js/contextPanel.js` replaces the permanent tab bar + always-visible accordion sections with one selection-driven panel ŌĆö CardDesigner / PageDesigner / StickerStudio / WorkspaceBuilder are mounted exactly as before (untouched internally) and keep doing all the real work; ContextPanel only (a) hides the tab bar + each section's accordion chrome via a `context-panel-mode` CSS class, and (b) toggles which existing `[data-card-section]` / tab-content is visible, driven by a small hook added to `js/app.js`'s existing `_setSelectedTextElement`/`_setSelectedSceneElement`/`showSlide`. Nothing selected shows Representation info + Change Representation + a Caption/Quote editor (Museum Gallery's existing Title/Artist/Age/Date or Quote/Attribution fields, rebuilt as simple bound inputs since the original WorkspaceBuilder-managed controls live inside a section this view doesn't reparent from) + a reused Page Background colour control + Add a Sticker (temporarily reveals the existing Sticker Studio tab). Two spec states have no independent hit-target in the current architecture and were deliberately simplified rather than requiring new hit-testing: Artwork and Frame selection show together as one "Your Picture" view (Fit/Fill/Original/BiggerŌåöSmaller/Move plus Frame Look/Frame Style/Frame Variation ŌĆö all already inside CardDesigner's 'image' section, since Story-role pages have no SceneEngine scene element and the separate 'frame' ("Picture Holder") section only ever applies to Cover/Hook/End pages); "Replace Artwork" / "Crop / Rotate" are new, small, additive actions (`PictureStudio.open` reused as-is) since replacing an already-placed picture in place didn't exist before this sprint ŌĆö uploading always created a new page. Title/Description/Metadata selection is one grouped Caption editor in the default view rather than three independently clickable canvas fields.)
- Theme Driven Representations (Sprint 10.1 / TB-4.7 ŌĆö Studio no longer hardcodes any theme's Representations; `js/creationFlow.js` and `js/contextPanel.js` read them live off the active theme. A theme now carries a flat `supportedCreationTypes` array (sibling to `layouts`/`frameVariations`, e.g. Museum Gallery `['artwork']`, Storybook Classic `['story']`) deciding which Creation Types it's offered under in Step 2 ŌĆö Creation Types themselves (`js/creationFlow.js`'s `CREATION_TYPES`) stay a small hardcoded list per this sprint's own scope, only themeŌåötype *compatibility* became data. A Creation Type with zero compatible registered themes shows "Coming Soon" immediately (no empty theme grid) instead of a fabricated placeholder theme object. Each theme's own `representations` array (Museum Gallery: Showcase/Portrait/Quote, unchanged behaviourally from 9.6/9.7's `theme.layouts` ids) is what Step 3 and "Change Representation" render ŌĆö each entry's `id`/`name`/`description`/`thumbnail`/`supportedCreationTypes`/`layout`/`defaultFrame`/`defaultLayerPack`/`background`/`actions` (┬¦8 of `docs/THEME_PROJECT_SPEC.md`); `actions` (`editCaption`/`editQuote`) is what `js/contextPanel.js` now checks instead of a hardcoded `layout==='quote'` test to decide which field group to show. Theme Builder gained an optional `representations/` folder (validated ŌĆö duplicate ids, `layout`/`defaultFrame` reference checks ŌĆö and compiled into `theme.representations`, mirroring `layouts/`/`frames/`/`layer-packs/` exactly); `js/themeEngine.js`'s zip-import path collects the same folder on import. `docs/VTHEME_PACKAGE_SPEC.md` documents the compiled shape. Verified end-to-end including a literal "rename a Representation on the live theme object, watch Studio's UI update with zero code changes" proof ŌĆö the sprint's own success metric, exercised directly.)
- Official Theme 001 ŌĆö Museum Gallery (Sprint 10.2 ŌĆö authoring only, no Studio/Theme Builder/Compiler/Theme Engine/Context Panel/runtime redesign. Museum Gallery is removed entirely from `js/themeRegistry.js`'s `OFFICIAL_ARTWORK_THEMES` array ŌĆö it no longer exists as in-code Studio data at all ŌĆö and re-authored as a real Theme Project at `theme-projects/MuseumGallery/` (manifest.json/metadata.json/theme.json + `layouts/`/`frames/`/`layer-packs/`/`representations/`, every field value transcribed unchanged from the removed in-code entry). Theme Builder loads/validates/compiles it with zero errors into `themes/MuseumGallery.vtheme` (replacing the older Sprint-9.6 zip-format file with the canonical flat `{manifest,theme,assets}` package ŌĆö see TB-4.6/TB-4.7). Trimmed to exactly the 3 Layouts (Landscape/Portrait/Quote) the 3 Representations (Showcase/Portrait/Quote) actually use ŌĆö Wide/Square/Full Bleed existed in the old in-code version but were never reachable through the Context Panel (Studio only ever initializes a page from a Representation), so they were not re-authored; no `assets/` folder, since every Frame field is an enum resolved to a drawn canvas routine, not a raster image. `theme.json`'s `supportedCreationTypes:["artwork","artwork-collection"]` ŌĆö "artwork-collection" is a forward-compatible reservation with no matching Creation Type card yet (Creation Types themselves stay Studio's small hardcoded list per Sprint 10.1's own scope). Museum Gallery now reaches Studio only through the ordinary Import Theme flow (`source:'imported'`, not `'official'`) ŌĆö proven end-to-end: fresh boot with nothing imported shows zero `museum-gallery` theme and "Artwork Showcase" renders Coming Soon; importing `themes/MuseumGallery.vtheme` makes Creation Flow Step 2/3 and Context Panel's "Change Representation" show Museum Gallery / Showcase-Portrait-Quote exactly as before, with zero Studio code changes required ŌĆö the sprint's own success metric, exercised directly rather than merely claimed.)
- Studio Arrival Experience (Sprint 11.0 ŌĆö implements the canonical "Studio Creation Journey V1" storyboard's first two screens; a restyle and re-flow of the Sprint 10.0/10.1 wizard, not a Workspace/Context Editing/Theme Engine/Theme Builder/Theme Registry/Publish Flow/Studio Runtime change. Three permanent canon documents were written before any code and were later corrected in place as the storyboard was clarified, rather than left stale: `docs/STUDIO_DESIGN_CANON.md` (visual/emotional identity ŌĆö a fixed warm-cream/paper-white watercolor palette independent of the app's own light/dark toggle, illustration style, spacing/interaction/motion philosophy, a "never look like Canva/PowerPoint/Figma/dashboards" list), `docs/STUDIO_CREATION_JOURNEY_V1.md` (Screen 1 ŌåÆ Screen 2 ŌåÆ Workspace ŌåÆ Workspace Context States ŌåÆ Publish, each stage's purpose/entry/exit/intent/objects-shown/hidden, product behaviour only), and `docs/STUDIO_SCREEN_2_INFORMATION_ARCHITECTURE.md` (Screen 2's full IA, v1.1); `js/creationFlow.js` implements those documents rather than redefining them. Screen 1 ("Choose What To Create") shows six storyboard-worded cards ŌĆö Tell a Story / Showcase My Artwork / Create Quotes / Write a Poem / Make a Greeting Card / More Ideas ŌĆö in a fixed 4-column grid (4+2 wrap, not an auto-fill grid) against a full-bleed illustrated "Story Meadow" (`.creation-scene` in `index.html`: sky gradient, sun glow, paper-grain SVG noise, drifting clouds, twinkling stars, rolling hills, grass, trees, swaying flowers, flying birds, fluttering butterflies, a drifting kite, a distant castle, and a wooden signpost reading "Your adventure starts here ŌÖź" ŌĆö pure CSS/emoji, no binary assets, `aria-hidden` and `pointer-events:none`). Screen 2 ("Choose Your Creative World") is a two-column master/detail layout, not a stacked wizard: `js/creationFlow.js`'s `_renderWorldScreen` builds a LEFT `.creation-flow-sources-panel` containing a **Vihu Worlds** row (official themes, horizontally scrolling with a scroll-chevron affordance) and a **World Library** row (imported themes, ending in an **Add New World** card) ŌĆö World Sources only, nothing else ŌĆö feeding a RIGHT **Selected World Preview** panel (large hero artwork, name, description, a "­¤ī┐ Begin With ­¤ī┐" Representation-card picker, Start Creating) as the single detail component every World ŌĆö regardless of source ŌĆö is read about and acted through; selecting any card from either row only ever repaints the Preview, never spawns a second picker. Add New World appears twice, both wired to the same import flow ŌĆö a header-level button beside the heading, and the World Library row's own last card ŌĆö reusing `ThemeEngine.importThemeFile` unchanged; a newly imported World is auto-selected and its Preview painted immediately, no restart, no reload. A Creation Type with zero compatible themes is never a dead end (closing the exact gap raised after Sprint 10.2): the Vihu Worlds row is simply omitted and the World Library row's Add New World card is always present, with the Preview showing a plain "add a world to get started" prompt instead of a separate "Coming Soon" screen ŌĆö there is no such screen. The Story Meadow scene stays mounted behind Screen 2, just faded (`.creation-flow-overlay.step2 .creation-scene{opacity:.55}`; the Screen-1-only signpost hides outright there instead of lingering faintly). The Context Panel's "Change Representation" shortcut is deliberately kept on its own lightweight render path (`_renderChangeRepresentationScreen`) ŌĆö Representation grid only, no World Sources panel, no Add New World ŌĆö since the active World is already fixed from the editor and Sprint 10.1's exact behavior there was out of this sprint's scope. Because the overlay's own background is no longer opaque (the meadow shows through it), the app header ŌĆö a sibling of `#app`, so untouched by the pre-existing `body.creation-flow-active #app{display:none}` rule ŌĆö gained its own `body.creation-flow-active` hide rule; the dev build-info footer instead got a raised `z-index` so it keeps showing crisply in the corner throughout the flow, per explicit product direction to keep build info visible while still in dev mode.)
- Product Asset System (Foundation ŌĆö a documentation and repository-organization sprint only; no Studio/Theme Engine/Theme Builder/runtime change. Establishes the permanent split between **Product Assets** (owned by VihuStudio, reusable across the whole product, versioned under `assets/` at the repo root) and **World Assets** (owned by an individual World, packaged only inside that World's own `.vtheme`, never stored under `assets/`) ŌĆö the two must never be duplicated into each other. `assets/` gained its full permanent folder structure ŌĆö `brand/`, `illustrations/{creation,source}/`, `environments/{story-meadow,open-sky,clouds,butterflies,flowers,paper-boats}/`, `ui/{buttons,cards,frames,textures,shadows}/`, `icons/{navigation,actions,status}/`, `stickers/`, `placeholders/` ŌĆö every folder carrying a README (purpose/ownership/expected asset types/naming convention/example usage), which doubles as that folder's git placeholder. Five canonical docs were added: `docs/PRODUCT_ASSETS.md` (the split itself + rules), `docs/PRODUCT_ILLUSTRATIONS.md` (reserves the six Creation Type illustrations ŌĆö Tell a Story/Showcase My Artwork/Create Quotes/Write a Poem/Greeting Cards/More Coming Soon ŌĆö as a permanent, reused-never-regenerated family, mapped to `js/creationFlow.js`'s existing `CREATION_TYPES` ids), `docs/ENVIRONMENTS.md` (documents Story Meadow's *existing* CSS/emoji implementation's palette/lighting/composition/motion as its permanent identity, and reserves Open Sky's identity for when it's built), `docs/ASSET_GUIDELINES.md` (illustration production style ŌĆö hand-painted/watercolour/storybook/paper-texture, never corporate/enterprise/dashboard/flat-SaaS ŌĆö cross-referenced with `docs/STUDIO_DESIGN_CANON.md` so the two never drift apart), and `docs/WORLD_ASSET_CONTRACT.md` (reserves an `assets/{hero,thumbnail,<representation-id>}.webp` packaging convention for Worlds, explicitly reconciled against the already-shipped `docs/THEME_PROJECT_SPEC.md`/`docs/VTHEME_PACKAGE_SPEC.md` contract ŌĆö today's real `thumbnail.png`/`preview.png`-at-project-root mechanism is left untouched, and the gap between it and this convention's ideal is named rather than glossed over). No artwork was created; the pre-existing `assets/icons/logo.png` was left in place untouched.)
- Screen 2 ŌĆö World Selection & Preview Experience (Sprint 11.1 ŌĆö implements Screen 2 only; no Workspace/Context Panel/Theme Engine/Theme Builder/Compiler/Publish/Creation Flow Step 1 change. Replaces the Sprint 11.0/11.1-prior click-to-select Page Style grid (checkmarks, a "­¤ī┐ Begin With ­¤ī┐" heading, a World name/description block) with the storyboard's actual model: **the Preview IS the layout selector**. `js/creationFlow.js`'s `paintPreview` now renders a compact World-identity heading (icon + name, non-interactive) followed by `.creation-flow-carousel` ŌĆö a horizontally scrollable, scroll-snap carousel with one large slide per entry in `theme.representations` (each slide showing that layout's own art/icon, name, description) ŌĆö with Start Creating living directly beneath it. There is no independent selection state: a scroll listener (`requestAnimationFrame`-debounced) computes the centred slide index from `scrollLeft`, drives the dot indicator and arrow-disabled state, and Start Creating always reads whichever index is current at click time, writing that slide's `layout` to `slide.metadata.layout` exactly as before ŌĆö swiping the carousel and pressing the button are the entire interaction, matching the sprint's explicit "no radio buttons, no dropdown, no second selection system" mandate. A World with zero Representations (Storybook Classic, today) still renders exactly one slide ŌĆö a synthetic `{__isDefault:true}` entry standing in for the World's own single layout ŌĆö so `Start Creating` always has something to act on and the carousel is never skipped; `_finish` treats that synthetic slide as "no representation" (unchanged behaviour). `_repCard` (the small click-to-select card) and `_renderChangeRepresentationScreen` (the Context Panel's "Change Representation" shortcut) are deliberately untouched ŌĆö a new, separate `_carouselSlide` builder serves only the Screen 2 Preview, so Change Representation keeps its pre-11.1 click-to-select behaviour exactly as Sprint 10.1 shipped it, since that surface is out of this sprint's declared scope. World Library's heading glyph corrected to ­¤ōÜ (from ­¤ō¢) to match the storyboard exactly. Verified end-to-end via Playwright, including the specific case of pressing Start Creating after arrow-navigating to a non-first slide and confirming the *visible* slide's layout ŌĆö not the first one ŌĆö is what gets applied.)
- Official World Platform ŌĆö Museum Gallery Reference Implementation (Sprint 11.2 ŌĆö establishes the permanent World Platform architecture: a World is content, Studio is a runtime, and the Studio never invents content a World's package doesn't declare. Museum Gallery's Theme Project source moved from `theme-projects/MuseumGallery/` to its permanent home `official-worlds/MuseumGallery/` ŌĆö the repository convention (`docs/THEME_PROJECT_SPEC.md` ┬¦0) every future Official World's source lives under ŌĆö and was recompiled through the unmodified Theme Builder tool with zero errors, producing a byte-identical `themes/MuseumGallery.vtheme` to before the move, proving the relocation didn't touch a privileged pipeline because there isn't one. Screen 2's Preview carousel (Sprint 11.1) had its one remaining fabrication removed: the synthetic single-slide `{__isDefault:true}` representation invented for a World with zero `theme.representations` is gone: `js/creationFlow.js`'s `paintPreview` now renders the carousel only when the package actually declares Representations, and for a World with none (Storybook Classic, a pre-existing legacy gap never touched by this sprint) shows no carousel and an honest "This world has no page styles to preview yet" message instead ŌĆö Start Creating still works, creating the page with no layout override, since that's a real, already-supported code path, not fabricated data. `docs/WORLD_ASSET_CONTRACT.md` gained a permanent Import Parity rule, quoted verbatim from this sprint's ticket: "An Official World is considered complete only when its compiled .vtheme package can be imported into a clean installation of VihuStudio and provides exactly the same creation experience as when shipped with the product" ŌĆö there is no runtime distinction between an Official World and an Imported World; the package is the product. A full codebase audit (`js/`, `renderer/`) confirmed zero hardcoded World/Theme special-casing of any kind ŌĆö every existing `switch`/`if` keyed on a string is a generic, theme-authorable enum (border design, paper, lighting, caption style, scene background, UI section id) that any World's package can set, never a specific World's id or name; the only "hardcoded" theme id anywhere is `storybook-classic` as the pre-existing default new-project Story Theme, an unrelated legacy concept predating and orthogonal to Artwork Theme/World identity. Verified end-to-end via Playwright: a fresh boot has zero `museum-gallery` anywhere until imported; importing `themes/MuseumGallery.vtheme` via Add New World renders exactly the 3 carousel slides the package declares (Showcase/Portrait/Quote, real descriptions, no `__isDefault` artifact anywhere in the DOM); the imported record's `source` is plain `'imported'` ŌĆö no privileged "official" flag; and Storybook Classic's zero-representation path shows the honest empty state with Start Creating still functional.)
- World Builder Foundation ŌĆö Product Reset (Sprint B1.0 ŌĆö retires the old Theme Compiler dashboard entirely and replaces it with **World Builder**, a creative, visual-first application per the approved World Builder Storyboard. `tools/theme-builder/` was renamed to `tools/world-builder/` (`git mv`, history preserved); its dashboard UI (`js/app.js`, `js/router.js`, `js/ui.js`, `js/state.js`, `js/eventBus.js`, `css/theme-builder.css`) is deleted outright ŌĆö not evolved, not preserved behind a flag. What survives, unchanged and audited to have zero dependency on the removed dashboard machinery, are the compile/validate engines as internal services under `tools/world-builder/js/services/` (`projectLoader.js`, `validator.js`, `builder.js`, and a trimmed `constants.js` keeping only `THEME_TYPES`/`DEFAULT_THEME_TYPE`/`LAYOUT_ASPECTS`/`LAYER_TYPES`/`LAYER_TARGETS` ŌĆö the dashboard-only `PAGES`/`EVENTS`/`VALIDATION_STATES`/`BUILD_STATES` enums retired with the UI that used them); `tools/world-builder/verify/goldenBuild.js` (all 30 assertions) now drives them directly through a new, non-user-facing `services-harness.html` instead of clicking dashboard buttons, proving the retirement didn't lose the regression coverage. Four permanent Architecture Locks are established in the new `docs/WORLD_BUILDER_ARCHITECTURE.md`: **LOCK 01** the Runtime (Studio) only ever consumes a compiled `.vtheme`, indifferent to whether it came from World Builder or a raw file (Sprint 11.2's Import Parity rule, unbroken); **LOCK 02** the Builder owns Projects (editable, Builder-owned, meaningless to Studio), the Runtime owns World Packages (immutable once built) ŌĆö nothing holds both roles; **LOCK 03** a New World is born valid ŌĆö the instant a creator picks a template, a complete World Project already satisfying the new `docs/WORLD_PROJECT_CONTRACT.md` is generated, no empty-project or "finish setup" state ever shown; **LOCK 04** the Builder is visual-first ŌĆö no JSON editors, no folder browsers, no developer terminology surfaced anywhere in Builder UI copy. `docs/WORLD_PROJECT_CONTRACT.md` defines a **World Project** as Builder-owned data (not a filesystem folder) persisted to `localStorage` ŌĆö deliberately isomorphic in shape to the existing Theme Project Contract (`README.md`/`manifest.json`/`metadata.json`/`theme.json`/`layouts/`/`representations/`/`frames/`/`layer-packs/`/`assets/`, plus a new per-project `docs/WORLD_SPEC.md` + `docs/WORLD_ASSET_SPEC.md`) so a future Build stage can feed it to the same unmodified `validator.js`/`builder.js` with no translation layer. Only two screens are implemented, both new: **Screen 1 (Welcome)** ŌĆö one primary Create New World CTA, a "My World Projects" list rendering live from the new `js/projectStore.js` (localStorage-backed, same pattern as `js/themeRegistry.js`'s `_persistImported`/`_loadImported`, explicitly no GitHub/cloud sync per this sprint's own instruction), and a static, non-interactive "Explore Worlds" section (Official/Community/Templates ŌĆö informational only, no behaviour behind it this sprint); **Screen 2 (Choose a Template)** ŌĆö six template cards (Artwork Gallery/Storybook/Quotes/Sketchbook/Greeting Cards/Blank World) rendered from the new `js/templates.js`, where clicking a card immediately calls `WorldTemplates.generate(id)` + `ProjectStore.create()` and returns to Screen 1 with the new draft visible ŌĆö no wizard, no dialog, no manual folder/JSON step. Each template's generated World Project carries real starter content matching its creative intent (e.g. Artwork Gallery: Showcase/Portrait/Quote representations mirroring Museum Gallery's own shape; Storybook: Cover/Story/Ending representations, entirely new illustrative content that does not touch the pre-existing in-code `storybook-classic` runtime theme; Blank World: zero representations, deliberately demonstrating the contract's own optionality). New `css/world-builder.css` matches the storyboard's warm/watercolor aesthetic (`docs/STUDIO_DESIGN_CANON.md` palette ŌĆö cream paper, rounded cards, gold reserved for the single primary action) ŌĆö no dashboard styling anywhere. Builder Workspace/Validation UI/Build UI/Publish/AI Assistance/Official World Authoring/Community Publishing are explicitly out of scope and not implemented. Verified end-to-end via Playwright: no developer terminology (JSON/manifest/schema/Validate/Build Status) appears anywhere in the rendered UI; all 6 templates generate a complete, contract-satisfying World Project (every required file present) and persist correctly to `localStorage`; `goldenBuild.js`'s pre-existing 30 assertions still pass unchanged, proving the retained services are untouched by the UI reset.)
- World Builder Workspace Foundation (Sprint B1.1 ŌĆö implements the permanent Builder Workspace from the approved World Builder Storyboard: Screen 3, the home of all World editing from here on. Two Screen 1/2 refinements land first: the "My World Projects" empty state changes from an absence-framed message to "Ō£© Your worlds will appear here. Create your first world to begin your journey."; the project card becomes a horizontal thumbnail+name+"draft ┬Ę edited Xh ago" list row wired to actually open a Project (previously inert); each of Screen 2's 6 template cards gains a short creator-facing blurb (e.g. Artwork Gallery: "Showcase paintings, drawings and photography beautifully."); and ŌĆö the Template Rule ŌĆö selecting a template no longer regenerates the Project and returns to Screen 1: it opens the Builder Workspace on the new Project immediately, since "the Builder edits a World Project, never a Template." The Workspace itself (`tools/world-builder/index.html`'s new `#wb-screen-workspace`, `css/world-builder.css`'s ~400 new lines, `js/worldBuilderApp.js`'s workspace half) is one screen with three permanent regions matching the storyboard exactly: a Header (World Project's own name ŌĆö "Untitled World" if unrenamed, never the template name ŌĆö + Draft Saved status; Preview/Settings/Save/overflow are present but inert this sprint); left Builder Navigation (Overview/Representations/Layouts/Frames/Layer Packs/Assets/Validation/Build/Publish ŌĆö nine fixed items, selecting one only swaps the Context Panel, never opens a new page, exactly like Studio's own object-selection model); a center Live Preview that never disappears regardless of Navigation state ŌĆö per LOCK 01 this is an illustrative mockup built from the Project's own data (icon/name/tagline/aspect-ratio/frame colour), not Studio's Runtime renderer reused inside the Builder; and one permanent right Context Panel reused by every state. Three real states are implemented: **Overview** (World Name/Tagline/Description/Publisher/Version/Creation Types/Thumbnail/Hero Image ŌĆö Thumbnail/Hero Image show placeholders with an inert "Change" button since Asset uploading is out of scope; all edits write through immediately and the Header's World Name updates live); **Representations** (list + "+ Add Representation," Name/Description/Default Layout/Default Frame/Layer Pack/Supported Actions ŌĆö `editCaption`/`editQuote` toggle chips ŌĆö for the selected one, changes repaint the Live Preview); **Layouts** (list + "+ Add Layout," Layout Name/Aspect/Holder Area [a static diagram, no functional drag this sprint]/Caption Position/Padding/Spacing/Alignment for the selected one, Aspect changes resize the Live Preview immediately). Frame editing, Layer Pack editing, Asset uploading, the Validation engine, the Build engine, Publishing, and AI assistance are explicitly out of scope and not implemented. - First Official World Platform Validation (Sprint B2.0 ŌĆö completes every remaining Builder Workspace state and proves the whole pipeline end-to-end by producing Museum Gallery as the first Official World authored entirely through World Builder, with zero manual JSON/folder editing. **Frames**: full CRUD (create/duplicate/rename/delete/reorder via `ProjectModel`) plus a property editor (Thickness/Padding/Inset/Border Color/Wall Tone/Shadow/Corner Radius/Default Margin), live in the Preview. **Layer Packs**: multiple named packs (Builder-only organization ŌĆö the compiled Runtime still merges every `layer-packs/*.json` file into one flat array per `docs/THEME_PROJECT_SPEC.md` ┬¦7, unchanged), a real Default Layer Pack control writing the previously-reserved `theme.json.defaultLayerPack` field, and a per-layer editor (Type/Target/Anchor/Position/Offset X-Y/Z-Index/Text Source/visibility/lock/reorder). **Assets**: entirely generated from new `docs/WORLD_ASSET_SPEC.md` (a canonical per-slot schema ŌĆö id/displayName/category/purpose/required/formats/recommendedDimensions/recommendedResolution/usedBy/previewType/validationRules) and its Builder-readable mirror `js/assetSpec.js` ŌĆö seven categories (Identity required; Frames dynamic per authored Frame; Textures/Decorations/Icons/Fonts/Backgrounds optional), real file upload (`FileReader` ŌåÆ data URI, the same embedding convention `builder.js` already used), live completion tracking. **Validation** and **Build** now run the real, unmodified `js/services/validator.js`/`builder.js` via new `js/projectCompiler.js` ŌĆö an adapter that populates the services' own global `projectLoader` singleton from an in-memory World Project (every `project.files[path]` becomes a real `Blob`), making good on the Sprint B1.0 promise that Build would need "no translation layer"; Validation reports pass/warning/error grouped by category, Build produces a genuine `{manifest,theme,assets}` package stored as `project.lastBuild`. **Publish**: Export Package and Official World both trigger a real download of exactly the Build-produced package; Community World is an honest inert placeholder. Overview gained World Id/Icon/Purpose/Mood fields and a real Creation Types toggle (all previously template-frozen or read-only), and README.md now regenerates from current Name/Tagline/Description instead of staying frozen at template-creation content; Layouts gained a Composition field (`below`/`right`/`quote`). Producing Museum Gallery for real surfaced and fixed four platform bugs, none cosmetic: Layouts were missing the required `name` field (`validator.js` rejects this, but nothing before this sprint had ever run real Validation to notice); a Frame Variation's presentation fields were flat instead of nested under `fields` per `docs/THEME_PROJECT_SPEC.md` ┬¦6 (compiled "successfully" but the runtime's resolver would never read them correctly); renaming a World in Overview never updated `theme.json.name`, failing validation the instant a creator renamed away from the template default; and several Workspace states re-rendered by appending instead of replacing (direct self-recursive calls skipped the dispatcher's own `innerHTML` clear), causing duplicate DOM fields whose edits silently landed on the wrong Layer. All four are fixed in `templates.js`/`projectModel.js`/`worldBuilderApp.js` and documented in new canonical `docs/FIRST_OFFICIAL_WORLD_REPORT.md`, alongside every contract enhancement, capability added, and the remaining honestly-named technical debt (no `theme.editor` block authoring, no `supportedFrames`/per-Representation `supportedCreationTypes` authoring, no `category`/`tags`/`bestFor`/`notRecommendedFor` editing yet ŌĆö none of which block a World from validating, building, publishing, or importing correctly). Museum Gallery's Theme Project source (`official-worlds/MuseumGallery/`) and compiled package (`themes/MuseumGallery.vtheme`) were regenerated from a mechanical dump of the Builder's own in-memory output (verified checksum-identical to a fresh Build) ŌĆö the only non-UI-driven step, disclosed as such, since a browser tool has no publish backend to place a file in the repository on its own. Verified end-to-end via Playwright: all 6 starter templates still generate contract-valid projects after the schema fixes; `goldenBuild.js`'s pre-existing 30 assertions still pass unchanged; a new 23-assertion suite exercises Frames/Layer Packs/Assets/Validation/Build/Publish including real file uploads and a real triggered download; and ŌĆö the sprint's own acceptance bar ŌĆö importing the Builder-produced `MuseumGallery.vtheme` into a clean Runtime shows zero `museum-gallery` anywhere before import, registers it immediately after with `source:'imported'` (no privileged flag), is discovered on Creation Flow Screen 2 with zero Runtime code changes, renders a Preview carousel of exactly the 3 authored Representations, resolves all 7 Frame Variations/5 Layer Pack entries/3 Representations through `ThemeEngine.getTheme()`, applies the correct authored Layout on Start Creating, and reaches `PublishStudio.open` through the ordinary Publish path with no special case.)

- Museum Gallery Authoring Feedback (Sprint B2.0.2 ŌĆö usability fixes drawn from real-world feedback authoring the first Official World through the Builder; no new screens/states, no architecture change, no Museum Gallery special-casing. **Overview**: World Id is now read-only (`_readOnlyField` ŌĆö auto-generated once at Project creation via `templates.js`'s `_slug(name) + '-' + _uid()`, never editable again, so nothing that already references it can break); the free-text Icon field is removed outright rather than reinterpreted (a future Icon, if any, comes from Category or an uploaded Asset, never free text). **Representations**: the Layer Pack field's help text now explains *why* every new World starts with a Layer Pack named "Basic" instead of only naming what a Layer Pack is. **Layouts**: gained a "Current Representation" banner reusing the existing shared `currentRepresentationId` (no new selection model) since a Layout is shared/reusable across Representations and creators had no way to know whose context they were editing in ŌĆö deliberately not a stricter ownership model, since that question (see A-005 below) isn't settled yet. **Center Preview**: the Preview modal's synthetic slide was silently resolving to `renderer/slideRenderer.js`'s own Story-runtime fallbacks ŌĆö an empty `handle` string falls through to the renderer's hardcoded `'@vihuplanet'` placeholder branding text (`_drawHandle`), and a null `themeOptions` resolved to `FALLBACK_OPTIONS` (`bookTitleVisibility:'show'`, `pageNumber:'bottom-right'`), so every World's Preview showed a stray `@vihuplanet` watermark, a footer named after the World itself masquerading as a book title, and an unrelated page number ŌĆö three pieces of invented Story-runtime furniture that don't belong to the World being authored. Fixed by passing an explicit `themeOptions` object with `bookTitleVisibility:'hide'`/`pageNumber:'hidden'`/`handleVisibility:'hide'`, so Preview shows only what the World itself defines (Frame/Layout/Layer Pack) ŌĆö a genuinely generic sample page. The modal's CSS was also restructured (new `.wb-preview-canvas-wrap` flex child, `.wb-preview-modal-box` at a fixed `88vh`) so the canvas always scales to fit the viewport with `overflow:hidden` guaranteeing no scrollbar ever appears, on any screen height. Two authoring findings are recorded as deliberately open in `docs/WORLD_BUILDER_ARCHITECTURE.md` rather than resolved on one data point: **A-005** (should Layout become owned by a single Representation, or stay independent/reusable as today) and **A-006** (should "Portrait," currently a Representation, instead be modeled as a Layout) ŌĆö both need more Official Worlds authored before deciding. A future **Visual Theme Composer** (interactive page anatomy, click-to-edit page layers) is noted as an explicit non-goal for any B2.x sprint. Verified via a new 15-assertion Playwright suite plus full regression (`verify_b201.js` 39/39, `verify_b20.js` 23/23, all 6 templates clean, `goldenBuild.js` 30/30, `verify_runtime_parity.js` all 8 phases).)

- Workspace Ergonomics (Sprint B2.0.4 ŌĆö layout-only sprint: no Builder logic, rendering logic, contracts, Project model, Runtime, Validation, Build, or Publish changes. Real authoring under Sprint B2.0.3 immediately exposed the problem: Runtime Preview shared a column with the Inspector, so as more Builder options were added the Inspector ŌĆö where a creator actually spends their editing time ŌĆö became cramped and required excessive scrolling. `.wb-workspace-body` becomes one CSS Grid (`nav`/`working`/`runtime`/`inspector` named areas) instead of nested flex columns: Navigation spans both rows (fixed, never scrolls); the top row splits Working View (center) and Runtime Preview (right, its own grid cell now instead of sharing one with the Inspector below it); the bottom row is the Inspector alone, spanning the full width beneath both ŌĆö substantially more usable space than the old ~340px shared column, and now the only region of the Workspace allowed to scroll at all. Working View and Runtime Preview switch their canvases from width-first to height-first fitting (`height:100%; max-width:100%; aspect-ratio:...`, the same fit-to-viewport technique the Sprint B2.0.2 Preview modal used) so neither ever scrolls now that each is a fixed percentage of the Workspace's height rather than sized to its own content; this surfaced a guide-label clipping bug (Sprint B2.0.3's guide labels floated above their box, fine when Working View owned a whole column's height, clipped once it didn't) fixed by moving every label inside its box's own edge instead. A new `_fieldRow()`/`_buildFieldGroup()` pair finally wires up the previously-unused Sprint B1.1 `.wb-field-row` CSS class to pair short, related fields side by side: Layouts (Aspect|Composition, Padding|Spacing, Caption Position|Alignment), Frames (Thickness|Padding, Inset|Corner Radius, Border Color|Wall Tone, Shadow|Default Margin), Representations (Default Layout|Default Frame), Overview (Publisher|Version, Purpose|Mood). `docs/WORLD_BUILDER_ARCHITECTURE.md` gained "The Workspace is one CSS Grid" documenting the mechanics; `docs/AUTHORING_FINDINGS.md` gained a Sprint B2.0.4 Builder Issues section. Verified via a new 25-assertion Playwright suite (grid geometry, no-scroll assertions on Working View/Runtime Preview, guide-label-not-clipped, every field pairing present, end-to-end edit still updates both surfaces) plus full regression across every prior sprint's suite, all passing unchanged.)
- Builder Workspace Polish (Sprint B2.0.5 ŌĆö visual-polish sprint on top of Sprint B2.0.4's grid: no new screens, no Workspace states, no architecture, contract, or rendering-pipeline change; Header/Navigation/Working View/Runtime Preview/Inspector regions stay frozen in position and role. Fixes two real, measured CSS defects rather than merely retuning numbers: (1) the `#wb-root` ancestor-padding bug ŌĆö `#wb-root`'s `max-width:1080px; margin:0 auto; padding:48px 32px 96px;`, meant only for Screens 1ŌĆō2's reading-column layout, was inherited by the always-`100vh` Workspace too, whose viewport-relative height doesn't shrink for an ancestor's padding ŌĆö so the Workspace's true footprint overflowed the viewport by exactly that padding while also losing width; the single largest contributor to "excessive whitespace." Fixed by moving that padding/max-width onto `.wb-screen-welcome, .wb-screen-templates` specifically, leaving `#wb-root` as bare `min-height:100%` ŌĆö the Workspace now measures exactly the full viewport rect. (2) A `flex:1` + `aspect-ratio` + `max-width:100%`-on-one-element distortion bug in Working View's and Runtime Preview's canvas wraps ŌĆö flex-grow resolves a definite height before `max-width` later clamps width, and the browser never retroactively shrinks the already-resolved height to match, producing real, measured stretching (Runtime Preview's canvas measured ratio 1.573 against a correct 1.25). Fixed with the same outer-sizing/inner-aspect-locked two-layer split the Sprint B2.0.2 Preview modal already used: a new `.wb-working-canvas-inner`/`.wb-runtime-preview-canvas-inner` element alone carries `aspect-ratio`+`max-width`+`max-height`, wrapped inside the pre-existing plain-flex outer wrap; `index.html` gained the matching wrapper `<div>`s, canvas element ids unchanged so no JS changed. `.wb-workspace-body`'s grid moved from Sprint B2.0.4's split to explicit `170px 1fr 380px` columns / `64% 36%` rows ŌĆö Navigation shrinks to only what icon+label+comfortable padding need, and the reclaimed width/height goes to Working View and Runtime Preview per the ticket's explicit P0 priority (not split evenly); Inspector's row-height share shrank in the trade but its architecture ŌĆö full-width, beneath both, independently scrollable ŌĆö is unchanged and it remains fully usable since it was already the one region allowed to scroll. Padding/gap tightened by a few px throughout Nav/Working View/Runtime Preview/Inspector as the "reduce gutters" P0 item; no component was stretched to fill space ŌĆö Working View's own column is now the widest, most prominent region on screen (satisfying "largest visual region"), while the empty margin around its smaller portrait-oriented page is the same relationship Figma's canvas has to a smaller artboard, not a defect, since stretching or cropping to eliminate it is explicitly prohibited. Adds basic Draft Management to the Welcome screen (the sprint's other P1 requirement): every project card gains Rename/Duplicate/Delete controls, each reusing an existing, already-real function rather than new persistence ŌĆö `ProjectModel.setIdentity(project, {name})` (the same call Overview's own World Name field already makes) for Rename, `ProjectStore.duplicate()`/`ProjectStore.remove()` (shipped in Sprint B2.0.1 for the Workspace header's overflow menu, never exposed here before) for Duplicate/Delete, `window.prompt()`/`window.confirm()` matching the header's own existing Delete confirmation pattern; Delete is architecturally incapable of touching a published Official Theme or exported `.vtheme` since `ProjectStore`'s `localStorage` key is a wholly separate persistence layer from `ThemeRegistry`'s imported-themes key or the `official-worlds/`/`themes/` folders ŌĆö never wired together, so the ticket's "must never be deleted automatically" constraint holds by construction. The project card changed from a `<button>` to a `role="button"` `<div>` with its own `keydown` handler (Enter/Space), since a native button cannot legally contain the three new nested action buttons ŌĆö the same pattern already used for Frame/Layout list rows, whose own controls likewise call `e.stopPropagation()`. Widening the card grid's `minmax()` floor from 220px to 320px was a companion fix, not a stylistic choice: the original value had no button-shaped content to make room for, and once Draft Management's controls were added the name column visibly collapsed and overlapped them ŌĆö verified via before/after screenshot. `docs/WORLD_BUILDER_ARCHITECTURE.md` gained a "Workspace Polish" section documenting both CSS bugs and the space reallocation; `docs/AUTHORING_FINDINGS.md` gained a Sprint B2.0.5 Builder Issues section. Verified via a new 20-assertion Playwright suite ŌĆö edge-to-edge Workspace geometry, both canvases holding exact 1080:1350 ratio at their new larger sizes, reduced Nav width, and full Rename/Duplicate/Delete/no-accidental-open coverage ŌĆö plus full regression across every prior sprint's suite and `goldenBuild.js`, all passing unchanged.)
- Builder Workspace Maturity (Sprint B2.0.6 ŌĆö the Workspace's final maturity pass before it freezes: no new screens, no new Workspace states, no architecture/contract/rendering-pipeline change; Header/Navigation/Working View/Runtime Preview/Inspector regions stay exactly where Sprint B2.0.4/B2.0.5 put them. **Property Editor grouping**: every state's field order was re-paired into a genuine property grid using the existing `_fieldRow()`/`_buildFieldGroup()` machinery ŌĆö Overview (World Name|Tagline, Publisher|Version, Purpose|Mood, Thumbnail|Hero Image as upload cards, Description last since it's the only multiline field), Representations (Name|Default Layout, Default Frame|Layer Pack, Supported Actions, Description), Layouts (Layout Name|Aspect, Composition|Caption Position, Padding|Spacing, Alignment|Used By ŌĆö "Used By" is a new compact readout surfacing the same Layout-reuse data the list above already showed per row), Frames (Frame Name|Wall Tone, Border|Corner Radius, Shadow|Inset, Padding|Margin, Thickness alone, Description last), and the Layer Packs Selected Layer form (Type|Target Container, Anchor|Position, Offset X|Offset Y ŌĆö Visibility/Lock were already inline icon buttons on each Layer List row, not stacked fields). The ticket's own illustrative Overview example named a "Category | Visibility" pair that doesn't exist anywhere in the World Project Contract or `ProjectModel`; rather than fabricate two new unused fields to match it, Overview's real pairing uses only fields Validation/Build/Runtime already read ŌĆö a deliberate, disclosed judgment call, not an oversight. **Assets** moved from stacked full-width rows to a real `.wb-asset-card-grid` (`_assetSlotRow` rebuilt from a horizontal row into a vertical card); **Build**'s two info boxes and **Publish**'s three options both moved from stacked elements to compact card grids via a new shared `_statCardGrid()`/`.wb-publish-grid`. **Builder Information Density**: the Sprint B2.0.1 What/Why/Do/Next guidance block is now a native `<details>`/`<summary>` (`_stateIntro()`), collapsed by default, one click away ŌĆö no JS toggle logic needed; short single-purpose status banners ("Previewing:", "Current Representation:") moved to a separate always-visible `.wb-info-banner` class so they're never mistaken for collapsible guidance. **Editing Confidence**: the static "Draft Saved" label is replaced by a real ­¤¤Ā Unsaved Changes / ­¤¤ó All Changes Saved indicator (`_setSaveState()`); the underlying `ProjectStore.save()` write stays synchronous and immediate inside `_persist()` (never debounced, so navigating away right after an edit can never lose it) ŌĆö only the *visible* return to "saved" debounces 600ms, so continuous typing shows one steady "Unsaved Changes" instead of flickering every keystroke; a synchronous save has no real "SavingŌĆ”" moment to show, so that sub-state was deliberately not fabricated. The Header Save button gained a `wb-save-btn-dirty` ring so the button itself communicates state, not just the badge. **Workspace Customisation**: three new sash-style resize handles (`#wb-resize-nav`/`#wb-resize-runtime`/`#wb-resize-inspector`) are real CSS Grid tracks (`.wb-workspace-body` gained `navsash`/`rtsash`/`tbsash` ŌĆö same nav/working/runtime/inspector region names, now with sash tracks threaded through), so a handle can never drift out of sync with the boundary it drags; each writes exactly one CSS custom property (`--wb-nav-w` clamped [180,280]px, `--wb-runtime-w` clamped to [25%,65%] of the combined Working+Runtime width, `--wb-inspector-h` clamped to [220px, 65vh]) via one shared `_wireResizeHandle()` mouse-drag driver. The chosen sizes persist to one Builder-wide `localStorage` key (`vihustudio.worldBuilder.workspaceLayout` ŌĆö deliberately a creator preference, not per-Project World data) and reapply automatically via `_applyWorkspaceLayout()` every time a Workspace opens; a new "Reset Workspace Layout" item in the header's three-dot menu clears that key and restores the shipped defaults with no reload. `docs/WORLD_BUILDER_ARCHITECTURE.md` gained a full "Property Editor grouping, Editing Confidence, and Workspace Customisation" section; `docs/AUTHORING_FINDINGS.md` gained a Sprint B2.0.6 section recording both the synchronous-save/no-fake-"Saving"-state decision and the not-fabricating-Category/Visibility decision as Builder Issues, plus an open Future Product Insight on whether workspace layout should ever become per-Project. Verified via a new 34-assertion Playwright suite (every field pairing, the collapsed/expandable guidance panel, the full dirtyŌåÆsaved cycle including a `localStorage` check proving the debounce never risks data loss, all three resize handles' drag direction/clamping/cross-reopen persistence, Reset Workspace Layout, the Assets/Build/Publish grids, and that Sprint B2.0.5's Draft Management is unaffected) plus full regression across every prior sprint's suite and `goldenBuild.js`, all passing unchanged.)
- Builder V2 ŌĆö Slice 1: Global Navigation, Scenes Library, Scene Configuration (implements `docs/BUILDER_V2_VISION.md` ŌĆö the first vertical slice of `tools/world-builder`'s reset onto Engine V2's object model per `docs/ENGINE_V2_CANON.md`/`docs/BUILDER_V2_BLUEPRINT.md`/`docs/BUILDER_V2_UX_PACKAGE.md`; not a redesign, an implementation of documents already frozen. **Global Navigation** moves to a real top bar (`#wb-global-nav`, World/Scenes/Validation/Build/Publish) structurally outside the workspace grid, replacing the old left Builder Navigation sidebar (Overview/Representations/Layouts/Frames/Layer Packs/Assets/Validation/Build/Publish) ŌĆö the corresponding CSS Grid nav column/sash retired along with it (`.wb-workspace-body` is now a 2-column grid, Working View + Runtime Preview, with only the Runtime and Inspector sashes remaining). Working View and Runtime Preview for a Scene are a small, self-contained canvas draw routine (`_drawSceneCanvas`) ŌĆö generic Holder placeholder chrome plus, in Working View only, a felt Safe Area guide ŌĆö deliberately **not** routed through `renderer/slideRenderer.js`, because no Engine V2 render pipeline exists for Scene/Canvas/Holder/Layer/Element in any frozen document; reusing the Engine V1 renderer for a shape it has no concept of would have been exactly the kind of silent architecture workaround this phase's brief prohibits. **A genuine, disclosed architectural gap, not silently bridged**: Validation/Build/Publish (`js/services/validator.js`/`builder.js`, `js/projectCompiler.js`) are completely unchanged this slice and still compile only `representations/`/`layouts/`/`frames/`/`layer-packs/` ŌĆö Scenes are new, additive authoring data with no compiled-package representation yet, because Engine V2 Canon defines an object model with no corresponding Engine V2 `.vtheme` format or Runtime support in any canon document. Every World template except Blank World now also seeds exactly one starter Scene (Blank World seeds none, matching its own "no assumptions" intent and exercising Blueprint ┬¦5's zero-Scene empty state). Representations/Layouts/Frames/Layer Packs' render functions are retained in `worldBuilderApp.js`, deliberately unreachable rather than deleted ŌĆö Frame selection returns inside the Place activity per Blueprint ┬¦8 once that activity is built, and that logic will be needed again shortly. Verified end-to-end via Playwright: create World ŌåÆ Scenes shows the seeded starter Scene ŌåÆ open it ŌåÆ Scene Header glance shows Portrait/Instagram Safe Area/1080├Ś1350 ŌåÆ selecting it populates Context Inspector with Aspect Ratio ŌåÆ changing to Landscape live-updates the glance, the Working View canvas, and the Runtime Preview canvas to 1350├Ś1080 ŌåÆ the activity switcher shows the honest Coming-in-the-next-sprint stub ŌåÆ "back to Scenes" returns to the Library ŌåÆ Add a Scene opens the 7-template picker and opens the new Scene ŌåÆ World/Validation/Build/Publish remain fully reachable and functionally unchanged from before this slice, with zero console errors throughout.)
- Builder V2 ŌĆö Slice 2: Place activity, real Holder authoring (implements Blueprint ┬¦8, the second vertical slice of the Builder V2 reset ŌĆö Place is no longer a stub. Selection is exactly Blueprint ┬¦6.1's rule: clicking a Holder in Working View selects it, switches the activity indicator to Place regardless of what was active a moment before, and populates Context Inspector ŌĆö a single `mousedown`/`mousemove`/`mouseup` driver wired once at module init (`worldBuilderApp.js`), reading `currentNav`/`currentSceneId`/`currentActivity` live rather than rebinding per render. **Position/Size** are draggable directly on the canvas (drag the Holder body to move, drag its bottom-right resize handle) and mirrored as Position X/Y % and Width/Height % sliders in Context Inspector ŌĆö both paths write the same fractional `holder.position`/`holder.size` and redraw live via a new `_redrawSceneCanvases()`, clamped so a Holder can never drag or resize past the Canvas edge. **Shape** (Rectangle/Rounded/Circle) and **Fit** (Fit/Fill/Original, Engine Canon ┬¦6's vocabulary) are real dropdowns (`js/services/engineSchema.js` gained `HOLDER_SHAPES`/`HOLDER_FITS`); Shape actually clips the canvas draw (`_drawHolderShapePath`, arc/rounded-rect/rect). **Padding** is a real, persisted field, disclosed honestly as cosmetically minor until a real photo replaces the placeholder. **Frame** ŌĆö confirmed living in Place, not Decorations, per Engine Canon ┬¦9's "Frame Element placed inside a Holder Layer" rule (Blueprint ┬¦8) ŌĆö is a card-grid picker of the World's existing `frames/*.json` (None + every Frame, swatched by `borderColor`); choosing one now visibly changes the Holder's rendered border colour/thickness on both Working View and Runtime Preview. - Engine V2 ŌĆö the native Runtime, first real implementation (`docs/ENGINE_V2_SCENE_MODEL.md` ┬¦5/LOCK V2-04's architectural decision ŌĆö Validation/Runtime/Build/Publish operate directly on the canonical Scene Model, no translation layer ŌĆö now has code behind it. New `tools/world-builder/js/services/engineRuntime.js` (`window.EngineV2Runtime`) is a small, generic module reading only a canonical Scene object (`scenes/<id>.json`'s exact shape, Scene Model ┬¦2/┬¦3) plus one injected `resolveFrame` callback for the model's one cross-reference (a Holder's Frame Theme Asset id) ŌĆö it never touches `window.ProjectModel`, `currentProject`, or any other Builder-only global, so it is callable from Working View, Runtime Preview, a Scene Library thumbnail, or a future non-Builder host with zero code change. `load(scene, resolveFrame)` performs Engine Canon ┬¦5 pipeline steps 1-3 (resolve the Canvas frame's pixel Size via `EngineSchema.aspectInfo`, walk `scene.stack` into an ordered, paint-ready graph); `render(ctx, graph)` performs step 4 (paint the Scene Stack bottom to top ŌĆö Holder placeholder chrome + Frame border, Decoration fill/glyph, Text word-wrap ŌĆö gating only on `visible`, per Engine Invariant 22, exactly as Engine Canon ┬¦5 step 5 specifies a published render must). `tools/world-builder/js/worldBuilderApp.js`'s `_drawSceneCanvas` ŌĆö previously a Builder-only canvas routine, explicitly disclosed in Slice 1's own report as deliberately *not* a Runtime ŌĆö now delegates its actual painting to `EngineV2Runtime.load`/`.render`, keeping only genuinely Builder-only authoring chrome as a thin wrapper on top (the felt Safe Area guide, selection outlines, the Holder resize handle ŌĆö none of which a published render would ever show, Engine Canon ┬¦5 step 5). This means Working View and Runtime Preview, Builder V2's own two rendering surfaces, are now proof this Runtime is real rather than theoretical: every Scene a Theme Author authors already renders through it today. `docs/ENGINE_V2_SCENE_MODEL.md` ┬¦7's open item on Holder Layers/Content Layer remains exactly as open as before ŌĆö this Runtime renders a Holder's placeholder chrome only, since Builder V2 still authors no independent Holder Layer stack to render instead. Verified via Playwright: a hand-built Scene object fed directly to `EngineV2Runtime.load`/`.render` with no Builder involvement paints correctly (a fill Layer's colour reads back from `getImageData`); every existing Working View/Runtime Preview interaction (drag a Holder, add a Decoration/Text, pick a Frame, change Aspect Ratio) still renders pixel-identically through the new path; zero console errors.)
- Builder V2 ŌĆö Workspace column reorder (explicit product amendment): the permanent three-column order changes from Working View | Runtime Preview | Context Inspector to **Working View | Context Inspector | Runtime Preview** ŌĆö Context Inspector now sits beside Working View since editing the current selection is the higher-frequency action, Runtime Preview moves to the smallest, rightmost column reflecting its lower-frequency "what will the reader see" role. Deliberately a separate, synchronous engine from `js/services/validator.js` (Engine V1, which round-trips through the `projectLoader` Blob singleton) ŌĆö no translation layer, per LOCK V2-04 ŌĆö its own "Scenes (Engine V2)" report renders in the Validation Context Inspector alongside, never merged into, the existing "World Contract (Engine V1)" category list. **Build metadata restored**: `tools/world-builder/build-info.json`/`js/buildInfo.js` gain `phase`/`milestone`/`slice` fields (falling back to the older `sprint`/`task` naming) so the Workspace footer reflects the current Engine V2 slice; following this repository's own established `chore(build): pin build-info to Sprint X commit` convention (a small follow-up commit referencing the real just-made commit SHA, since a commit cannot self-reference its own hash in the same commit), this becomes the standard per-slice closing step going forward. - Engine V2 ŌĆö Build and Publish (compiling and sharing the canonical Scene Model, per `docs/ENGINE_V2_SCENE_MODEL.md` ┬¦5/LOCK V2-02/V2-04). New `tools/world-builder/js/services/engineBuilder.js` (`window.EngineV2Builder`) is a pure function from a validated World's Scene Model to a package ŌĆö requires `EngineV2Validator` to report zero errors first (mirroring Engine V1's own established Build-requires-Validation convention), then produces a flat JSON envelope (`{format:'engine-v2-world-package', formatVersion, manifest, metadata, theme, scenes, frames, builtAt}`) ŌĆö World identity fields unchanged in shape from Engine V1 (Scene Model ┬¦2), every Scene exactly as authored, every Frame a Holder might reference (the model's one cross-reference). Deliberately not named or shaped like `.vtheme` (`<id>.v2world.json` instead) since Engine V1's and Engine V2's compiled formats are not interchangeable and sharing a name would misleadingly suggest otherwise (LOCK V2-04). No `assets/` folder ŌĆö every Frame field is an enum resolved to a drawn canvas routine today, not a raster image, the same reasoning Museum Gallery's own Engine V1 package used. The Build screen gained a "Scenes (Engine V2)" section (its own stat cards, its own "­¤Ä¼ Build Scene Package" button, storing the result as `project.lastSceneBuild` ŌĆö a dataURL, matching Engine V1's own `project.lastBuild` shape so `_downloadDataURL` works identically for both) ahead of the existing, untouched "World Package (Engine V1)" section. The Publish screen gained a matching "Scenes (Engine V2)" section offering only **Export Scene Package** ŌĆö deliberately just a download, since no Engine V2 Runtime exists outside this Builder yet for an "Official Themes"-style install to target (LOCK V2-04's native Runtime is implemented as Working View/Runtime Preview's own rendering path, not yet as a standalone reader-facing consumer); this is a disclosed gap, not an oversight, and matches Scene Model ┬¦5's own "sharing mechanics are unchanged in *kind*" framing ŌĆö Export exists in both engines' Publish, Official/Community do not yet in Engine V2's. Both new sections read/write only `project.lastSceneBuild`, never `project.files` directly, matching Engine V1 Publish's own "never read the editable Project" discipline (Sprint B2.0.1). Verified via Playwright: Build produces a real, well-shaped package (`format`/`formatVersion`/scene count/frame count all correct); Publish's Export button triggers a real file download with the correct filename; the Engine V1 Build/Publish sections remain fully functional and unaffected; zero console errors throughout. With this, all six items Engine V2 needed ŌĆö Workspace alignment, Runtime, Renderer, Validation, Build, Publish ŌĆö are implemented against the canonical Scene Model with no translation layer and no parallel architecture, per LOCK V2-04.)
- Authoring Validation AV-001 ŌĆö Working View/Runtime Preview adopt the Scene's own Aspect Ratio (a real authoring bug found while beginning to author the official Museum Theme in Builder V2, not an Engine/Runtime issue ŌĆö Engine Canon ┬¦4 already correctly ties Canvas geometry to the Scene's Aspect Ratio, and `EngineV2Runtime`/`_drawSceneCanvas` already correctly resized the canvas's own pixel buffer, `canvasEl.width`/`.height`, per Scene ŌĆö see Sprint "Engine V2: the native Runtime"). The bug was purely a CSS/layout omission: `.wb-working-canvas-inner`/`.wb-runtime-preview-canvas-inner` (the canvas's own parent box, which the canvas fills via `width:100%;height:100%`) carried a hardcoded `aspect-ratio: 1080 / 1350`, so a Landscape/Square/Quote Scene's correctly-sized bitmap was silently stretched to fill a portrait-shaped box ŌĆö Working View and Runtime Preview looked permanently portrait no matter what Aspect Ratio was selected, while the underlying Holder/Layer geometry was already correct. Fixed with one line in `_drawSceneCanvas` (`canvasEl.parentElement.style.aspectRatio = graph.width + ' / ' + graph.height`), set from the same `EngineV2Runtime.load` graph already used to size the canvas buffer ŌĆö the stylesheet's `1080/1350` value is now only a before-first-render fallback, overridden inline on every real draw. No Engine V2/Scene Model/architecture change of any kind; a one-line authoring-surface correctness fix. Verified via Playwright: switching Portrait ŌåÆ Landscape ŌåÆ Square ŌåÆ Quote ŌåÆ Portrait each produces a Working View/Runtime Preview box whose on-screen aspect ratio matches the Scene's own (0.8 / 1.25 / 1.0 / 0.8), Safe Area guide recalculates correctly for each, and Holder click-select + drag-to-move continue working correctly under a non-portrait Aspect Ratio. Zero console errors.)
- Authoring Validation AV-002 ŌĆö the Scene becomes a first-class selectable object (a real selection/navigation gap found in the same authoring session as AV-001, again not an Engine/Runtime/architecture issue ŌĆö Scene was always a real Context Inspector state, `currentInspectorTarget === 'sceneConfig'`, reachable via the Scene Header's own glance; the gap was that Working View itself had no path to it). Two call sites fixed, both in `tools/world-builder/js/worldBuilderApp.js`: (1) `_openScene` (fired both when a brand-new Scene is created and when reopening one from the Scenes Library) now defaults `currentInspectorTarget` to `'sceneConfig'` instead of `null` ŌĆö configuring the Scene's own shape is the first authoring action a Theme Author sees, not an immediately-selected Holder; (2) the shared `mousedown` handler's "nothing hit" branch ŌĆö previously it only cleared an existing Holder/Layer selection back to `null` when one was active, otherwise doing nothing ŌĆö now unconditionally selects Scene Configuration, making the empty Canvas area the natural, always-available hit target for the Scene itself, mirroring exactly how clicking a Holder/Decoration/Text selects that object (Blueprint ┬¦6.1).
