Zero console errors, no Engine V2 changes.)
- Authoring Validation AV-003 ŌĆö the complete Holder presentation pipeline (Frame's full field set, plus Fit and Padding) actually renders (real Builder-side bugs found authoring the official Museum Theme's White Museum Frame ŌĆö not an Engine/Scene-Model/architecture issue; every property persisted correctly all along). **Root cause 1 ŌĆö Frame silently never applied:** `EngineV2Runtime`'s `_paintHolder` (`js/services/engineRuntime.js`) calls its injected resolver as `graph.resolveFrame(holder.frame)` ŌĆö passing the Frame *id* ŌĆö but `worldBuilderApp.js`'s `_holderFrameFields` (the function wired in as that resolver) was written to accept a *Holder object* and read `.frame` off it; called with a plain id string, `arg.frame` is always `undefined`, so the resolver returned `null` for every Holder regardless of which Frame was picked. Fixed by changing `_holderFrameFields`'s parameter to the id it's actually called with ŌĆö the Runtime's own call site was correct all along. **Root cause 2 ŌĆö Fit and Padding never triggered a redraw:** unlike every other Holder field in `_renderHolderPanel`, the Fit `<select>` and Padding `<input type=range>` handlers called `updateHolder`+`_persist()` but never `_redrawSceneCanvases()`. Fixed by adding the same call already present on every sibling field. **Root cause 3 ŌĆö the deeper, systemic one, found only after a direct follow-up question ("verify every Frame property end to end; find the common point, not the individual symptoms"):** `_paintHolder` had only ever consumed 2 of the 8 fields the Frames screen actually authors (`borderColor`, `frameThickness`) ŌĆö `wallTone`, `cornerRadius`, `shadow`, `inset`, `matWidth`, and `defaultMargin` all persisted correctly via `ProjectModel.setFrameFieldValue` but had no code path into either rendering surface at all, redraw bugs aside. `_paintHolder` is that common point, not any one field's own handler. Rewrote it as a set of concentric filled bands, outside in ŌĆö wall margin (`defaultMargin`+`inset`, filled `wallTone`) ŌåÆ frame border (`frameThickness`, `borderColor`) ŌåÆ mat (`matWidth`, a fixed neutral tone) ŌåÆ content (the Holder's own `padding`, Engine Canon ┬¦6) ŌĆö each via one shared `_band(insetPx, color)` helper that also shrinks `cornerRadius` by the running inset so every band's outer edge meets the previous band's inner edge exactly, with no gap and no overlap (an earlier centered-stroke version of the border band left a visible unstyled gap before the mat; replacing the stroke with a filled band removed the half-thickness bookkeeping that bug came from). `shadow` (`none`/`soft`/`floating`/`gallery`) is applied once, only to the outermost band, via real `ctx.shadowColor`/`shadowBlur`/`shadowOffsetY` presets. **Fit's visual meaning implemented for the first time**, matching the three-way vocabulary Engine Canon ┬¦6 already names (`fit`/`fill`/`original`), applied to the placeholder glyph since no Primary Element/Content Layer is separately authored yet (Scene Model ┬¦7 open item 1, unchanged). Verified via Playwright: Frame NoneŌåÆClassic White changes the rendered border colour immediately in both Working View and Runtime Preview, identical in both; every one of the 8 Frame fields (wallTone, defaultMargin, inset, cornerRadius, shadow, matWidth, frameThickness, borderColor) set to a distinct extreme value produces its own correctly-ordered, correctly-bounded band, sampled pixel-by-pixel across the transition from the Holder's outer edge inward with no gaps; Fit fitŌåÆfillŌåÆoriginal all persist and visibly resize the placeholder; Padding smallŌåÆlarge visibly insets the placeholder; Holder/Scene selection (AV-002) and Aspect Ratio switching (AV-001) both still work unaffected; zero console errors; no Engine V2/Scene Model changes.)
- Authoring Validation AV-004 ŌĆö Working View becomes an adaptive construction workspace instead of a duplicate of Runtime Preview (a Builder UX finding, not an Engine/rendering issue ŌĆö Runtime Preview was already correct and unaffected; Working View simply carried zero authoring-specific affordances beyond the pre-existing Safe Area guide and selection outline, so it read as a second, redundant "what the reader sees" surface rather than a construction tool). **Product principle established**: Runtime Preview is frozen ŌĆö always exactly the published reader output, selection-independent; Working View is allowed to adapt to whatever is currently selected, showing Builder-only guides that never serialize, never publish, never affect exports, and never touch Engine V2 rendering. **Implementation, entirely inside the existing frozen architecture**: `engineRuntime.js`'s `_paintHolder` already computed a Holder's Frame band geometry (wall margin ŌåÆ border ŌåÆ mat ŌåÆ content, AV-003) inline; that geometry was extracted into one shared, read-only function, `_holderInsets(holder, fields, graph)`, so the paint routine and any future geometry query are guaranteed to agree ŌĆö a guide computed from separately-reimplemented math could otherwise silently drift out of sync with what's actually drawn. A new public query, `EngineV2Runtime.holderBands(holder, graph)`, reuses `_holderInsets` to return the same band rectangles (`outer`/`border`/`mat`/`content`) as plain data, with no drawing side effect ŌĆö added to the module's existing `{load, render, rectFor}` export as `holderBands`, still a pure function of the canonical Scene Model plus the injected Frame resolver, nothing new for `EngineV2Runtime` to know about Builder UI. `worldBuilderApp.js` gained `_drawHolderConstructionGuides(ctx, holder, graph, canvasWidth)`, called only from `_drawSceneCanvas`'s pre-existing `opts.interactive` branch (Working View only, never Runtime Preview) when a Holder is selected ŌĆö it calls `EngineV2Runtime.holderBands()` and draws dashed, labelled boundary lines ("Wall ŌåÆ Frame", "Frame ŌåÆ Mat" or "Frame ŌåÆ Artwork" when there's no mat, "Artwork") directly on top of the identical `EngineV2Runtime.render()` output already painted by both surfaces, deduplicating adjacent bands that share identical bounds (e.g. zero-width mat) so a redundant line is never drawn. Scene selection's own construction context (composition/safe area) was already served by the pre-existing Safe Area guide from AV-001/Slice 1 and needed no new code. This is deliberately scoped to visual, non-interactive guide lines ŌĆö not drag-to-edit handles on the guide boundaries themselves ŌĆö since the ticket's own "exact affordances are a Builder decision" left room to choose the lower-risk option for this slice; a future slice could make these boundaries draggable without changing this slice's architecture. Verified via Playwright: selecting a Holder shows correctly-labelled dashed band-boundary guides in Working View only; deselecting back to Scene Configuration (AV-002) removes them; a pixel-level comparison of Runtime Preview's canvas (`getImageData` sampled across a 20├Ś20 grid) is byte-identical before and after Holder selection, proving the guides never bleed into the reader-facing surface; full regression across AV-001/AV-002/AV-003/Slice/Validation/Build/Reorder test suites all pass unchanged; zero console errors; no Engine V2/Scene Model/Runtime Preview rendering changes.)
- Authoring Validation AV-005 ŌĆö Runtime Preview stays project-scoped instead of switching to a reusable-asset editor's own specimen (a Builder product bug found authoring the Museum Theme's Frames, not an Engine/rendering issue ŌĆö correcting, not walking back, AV-004's own "Runtime Preview is frozen/project-scoped, Working View is editor-scoped" contract, which `_renderPreview()`/`_redrawSceneCanvases` hadn't actually honoured for every Builder screen). **Root cause**: `_renderPreview()` (`worldBuilderApp.js`) picked one rendering mode for *both* Working View and Runtime Preview based solely on `currentNav` ŌĆö for every nav other than `'scenes'` (Frames/Layouts/Representations/Layer Packs/etc.) it built a synthetic specimen slide via `_buildPreviewSlide`/`SlideRenderer.render()` and painted it into both canvases, so entering "Manage Frames" (Slice 2's own "manage the full shelf" bridge, which deliberately keeps `currentSceneId` set so "ŌåÉ Back to Scene" can return) replaced Runtime Preview's Museum Scene render with a standalone Frame specimen ŌĆö Working View becoming the specimen editor was correct, Runtime Preview following it along was the bug. Compounding it, `_redrawSceneCanvases(sceneId)` unconditionally early-returned whenever `currentNav !== 'scenes'`, so even a manual redraw request while a Scene was open behind another editor was silently dropped. **Fix, entirely inside frozen architecture, no second renderer**: a new `_activeSceneForRuntimePreview()` reads `currentSceneId` independent of `currentNav`; `_renderPreview()` now paints Runtime Preview via the existing `_drawSceneCanvas(runtimePreviewCanvas, activeScene, {guides:false, interactive:false})` ŌĆö the exact same Engine V2 pipeline Scenes nav already uses ŌĆö whenever a Scene is active, regardless of which nav/editor Working View shows instead, and only falls back to the legacy `SlideRenderer` specimen for Runtime Preview when no Scene is open at all (Overview/Representations/etc. on a project with zero Scenes, unchanged prior behaviour); Working View's own per-nav specimen/identity-card logic is completely untouched, since AV-004's "Working View is editor-scoped" half of the contract was never wrong. `_redrawSceneCanvases` now redraws Runtime Preview whenever `currentSceneId` matches, and additionally redraws Working View's own Scene-editor canvas only when `currentNav === 'scenes'` ŌĆö same split. **A second, related bug surfaced and fixed in the same pass**: `_renderFramesPanel`'s field handlers only called `_renderPreview()` after 3 of its 8 Frame fields (Wall Tone, Border Color, Frame Thickness) ŌĆö Corner Radius/Shadow/Inset/Padding(Mat Width)/Default Margin persisted via `setFrameFieldValue` but never triggered a repaint of either canvas, the identical "missing redraw call" class of bug AV-003 found and fixed for the Holder panel's Fit/Padding fields; added the same `_renderPreview()` call to all 5 missing handlers so every Frame property updates both the Working View specimen and the live Runtime Preview Scene immediately, per this ticket's own acceptance criteria. `EngineV2Runtime`/`engineRuntime.js` and the Scene Model are completely unchanged ŌĆö the fix lives entirely in which canvas `worldBuilderApp.js` chooses to paint and when, reusing the same `_drawSceneCanvas`/`EngineV2Runtime.load`/`.render()` calls Scenes nav already made. Verified via Playwright: selecting a Holder, assigning it a Frame, then opening Manage Frames shows Working View switch to the Frame specimen editor while Runtime Preview's canvas stays pixel-identical (still the Museum Scene, framed Holder and all); editing Border Color and ŌĆö critically ŌĆö Corner Radius (previously silently dead) both now visibly update Runtime Preview's rendered Scene live; full regression across AV-001/AV-002/AV-003/AV-004/Slice/Validation/Build/Reorder suites all pass unchanged; zero console errors; no Engine V2/Scene Model changes, no serialization/export changes.)
- Builder Authoring Polish ŌĆö AP-001/AP-002/AV-006 (a Builder-usability-only pass, no architecture/Engine V2/Scene Model change; all three items found or requested while continuing Museum Theme authoring after AV-005). **AP-001 ŌĆö developer language removed from Builder UI copy**: every Context Inspector panel string that leaked internal terminology to the author is rewritten in plain product language ŌĆö the Decorations "Add a Decoration" help text (`Engine Canon ┬¦9... a future slice, not yet built here` ŌåÆ `Choose a decoration to place in your scene`, the ticket's own literal example), the `scenes` STATE_GUIDANCE entry (`Engine V2 Canon ┬¦0`/`arrive in a following slice` ŌåÆ plain wording matching that Place/Decorations/Text are already real, not upcoming), Scene Configuration's heading/help text (`Engine V2 Canon ┬¦4`/`Vision ┬¦2`/`Blueprint ┬¦7` ŌåÆ plain wording), the Place panel heading (`Blueprint ┬¦6.2, ┬¦8` ŌåÆ plain wording), and ŌĆö the largest offender, found by grepping every `textContent`/`innerHTML` UI string rather than stopping at the ticket's one example ŌĆö the Validation/Build/Publish panels' own permanent section headings literally read `Scenes (Engine V2)` / `World Contract (Engine V1)` / `World Package (Engine V1)` verbatim in the rendered UI, plus a Publish note disclosing `no Engine V2 Runtime exists outside this Builder yet to install it into` (an implementation-status admission the ticket explicitly forbids); all renamed to plain `Scenes` / `World Contract` / `World Package` (the two package kinds stay distinguishable by name alone, since one produces a Scene Package and the other a World Package) and the Publish note reworded to `Download the built Scene Package to your computer to back it up or share it`. (see the Sprint 11.0 "Studio Arrival Experience" build-info footer decision), not Builder authoring-panel copy, so it's outside this ticket's "Builder should present itself as a finished creative product" scope. **AP-002 ŌĆö emoji panel-title headings replaced with inline SVG icons**: `assets/icons/{navigation,actions,status}/` were confirmed to be empty placeholder folders (Product Asset System sprint reservations, no actual icon files), and emoji is genuinely the Builder's own consistent, pervasive icon language elsewhere (Global Nav, Activity switcher, row-control buttons, stub panels, Publish cards) ŌĆö so rather than fabricate a full replacement icon set unilaterally (a real design decision the ticket's own example didn't fully specify), this narrowed to the specific large panel-title emoji the ticket's example pointed at: a new `ICONS` lookup (`worldBuilderApp.js`) with three small inline `<svg>` glyphs (picture/sparkle/pencil, `currentColor` stroke, no binary assets) for Place/Decorations/Text, `_heading()` gained an optional third `iconSvg` parameter, and the three permanent pane headings (Working View/Context Inspector/Runtime Preview, hardcoded in `index.html`) got matching inline SVGs (frame/magnifying-glass/eye) ŌĆö Nav bar, Activity switcher, and row-control glyphs are unchanged emoji, a disclosed scope decision, not an oversight. **AV-006 ŌĆö text drag movement had an invisible barrier, root cause found and fixed**: a text Scene Layer's declared `position`/`size` box (Scene Model ┬¦3's generic fractional-rect vocabulary, shared with Holder/Decoration) is, for text specifically, only ever a wrap-width and a creation-time placeholder height (`size:{w:0.7,h:0.15}` by default) ŌĆö completely decoupled from the layer's actual rendered extent, which depends on real word count and line-wrapping (`engineRuntime.js`'s `_paintLayer`/`_drawWrappedText`, top-down from the box's own top edge, never clipped to or centered within `size.h`). The Builder's drag-clamp (`Math.min(1 - obj.size.h, ...)`), hit-test (`_pointInHolder`), and selection-outline drawing all clamped/tested against that declared box, so a short line of text sitting in the default 15%-tall box could never be dragged closer than 85% down the Canvas, stopping visibly short of the actual Safe Area with an unstyled gap below the true glyphs ŌĆö exactly Blueprint's own "invisible movement barrier" framing. Fixed entirely inside the frozen architecture, matching AV-004's established pattern of adding a pure, read-only geometry query rather than a second implementation: `engineRuntime.js`'s wrap-loop was extracted into a shared `_wrapLines(ctx, text, maxWidth)` used by both `_drawWrappedText` (paint, unchanged output) and a new exported `textFootprint(ctx, layer, graph)` (query only, no drawing) that measures the real rendered line count/height and returns the *actual* footprint rect ŌĆö added to the module's existing `{load, render, rectFor, holderBands}` export. `worldBuilderApp.js` gained `_effectiveObjectRect(obj, kind, canvasEl)`, returning that measured footprint for text Layers and `null` otherwise (Holders/Decorations completely unaffected, since their declared rect already *is* what's drawn); `_pointInHolder` now accepts the object's kind + canvas element and hit-tests against the footprint when it's text, the drag-clamp's `Math.min(1 - obj.size.h, ...)` now clamps against the measured footprint's fractional height for text specifically, and the selected-Layer outline (`_drawSceneCanvas`'s interactive branch) traces the same footprint rather than the stale declared box. Verified via Playwright: dragging a short "New text" element toward the Canvas bottom now reaches yŌēł0.956 (previously hard-clamped at 0.85), landing flush with the true bottom edge in both Working View (selection outline hugging the actual glyph, no gap) and Runtime Preview identically; full regression across AV-001 through AV-005/AP-001/AP-002/Slice/Validation/Build/Reorder suites all pass unchanged; zero console errors; no Engine V2 rendering change (`render()`/`_paintLayer`'s pixel output is byte-for-byte the same ŌĆö only a new, additive, non-drawing query function was added) and no Scene Model change.)
- Project Card Representation ŌĆö Welcome screen shows the authored World thumbnail (a Builder usability fix found authoring the Museum Theme; no Engine V2/navigation/architecture change). `_projectCard`'s `.wb-project-thumb` (`tools/world-builder/js/worldBuilderApp.js`, the "My World Projects" list on Screen 1) unconditionally rendered `project.icon || '­¤īÄ'` as plain text ŌĆö it never checked whether the World had an authored `thumbnail.png` asset, even though the exact same `getAsset(project,'thumbnail.png')`-with-`<img>`-fallback pattern already existed one screen away in the Overview identity card (`_renderIdentityCard`), and the CSS (`.wb-project-thumb img{...}`, `overflow:hidden`) was already in place anticipating an image the JS never actually inserted. Fixed by reusing that identical pattern in `_projectCard`: when `ProjectModel.getAsset(project,'thumbnail.png')` returns a value, an `<img>` fills the thumb; otherwise the icon glyph placeholder renders exactly as before. Verified via Playwright: a World with an uploaded thumbnail shows the real image on its Welcome-screen card; a World with no thumbnail continues showing its emoji placeholder; full regression across every prior AV/AP/Slice/Validation/Build/Reorder suite passes unchanged; zero console errors; no Engine V2, Scene Model, export, or navigation changes.)
- Authoring Validation AV-007 / Builder Evolution EV-002 ŌĆö Holder Fit/Fill made visually meaningful via a Theme's own representative artwork (real Builder authoring findings, not Engine V2/Scene Model issues; investigated before assuming a cause, per the ticket's own instruction). **Root cause (AV-007)**: two compounding bugs in `_paintHolder`'s placeholder rendering (`engineRuntime.js`), not one. (1) `fill`'s glyph size was `Math.min(cw,chgt) * 0.55` ŌĆö always *smaller* than the content rect, so it could never overflow/crop against anything, reading as barely different from `fit`'s `0.3`. (2) Even fixed, an emoji glyph is a poor demonstration of crop behaviour ŌĆö a single small icon centred in a box can't show "cover vs. contain" the way a real photo does, since there's no edge-to-edge detail to visibly clip. **Fix**: `_paintHolder`'s content band is now clipped to its own content rect (previously only the outer Holder-shape clip existed, so a naively-enlarged glyph or image could spill onto the mat/border bands), and draws `graph.representativeImage` ŌĆö a real `Image`, when available ŌĆö via a new `_drawImageWithFit(ctx, img, rect, fit)` using genuine `object-fit` math (`fit`=contain, `fill`=cover-and-crop, `original`=native size), the same vocabulary the Engine V1 image viewer already uses for a real photo. The glyph fallback (no artwork authored at all) keeps working exactly as before except `fill`'s multiplier is corrected to `1.4` (genuinely larger than the content rect, so it now visibly clips at the corners too). **EV-002's resolution**: rather than fabricate a second "sample artwork" concept (the ticket's own explicit instruction ŌĆö `_sampleArtworkImage`, the generic gradient stand-in the legacy Engine V1 specimen path already uses, is untouched and unrelated), `worldBuilderApp.js` gained `_representativeArtworkImage(project, sceneId)`, which resolves the World's own authored Hero Image (`preview.png`, the higher-resolution source Overview's own "Hero Image" field uploads to) and falls back to Thumbnail (`thumbnail.png`) only if no Hero Image exists yet ŌĆö matching the ticket's own "prefer its original high-resolution source" instruction exactly; no technical constraint was hit, so no new asset concept was needed. Cached by data-URL (invalidates automatically on re-upload) and loaded asynchronously via a real `Image`, redrawing the Scene once decoded. `EngineV2Runtime.load(scene, resolveFrame, representativeImage)` gained one new optional third parameter, threaded onto the returned graph exactly like `resolveFrame` ŌĆö the Scene Model schema, the 4-step pipeline, and `render()`'s own signature are unchanged. Verified via Playwright: with a Theme's own Hero Image authored and no Frame assigned, `fit` shows the image letterboxed inside the Holder (background visible at all four content-rect corners, identical in Working View and Runtime Preview) while `fill` shows the image covering the Holder edge-to-edge with the overflow cropped (all four corners and centre pixel-match the image exactly) ŌĆö an unambiguous, easily-authored difference; full regression across every prior AV/AP/Slice/Validation/Build/Reorder/Project-Card suite passes unchanged; zero console errors; no Engine V2/Scene Model/export changes.)
- Authoring Validation AV-008 ŌĆö a real Builder workspace/navigation model, not an Engine or rendering issue (four findings from prolonged Museum Theme authoring). **(1) Resume last editing context**: `openWorkspace(project)` previously always reset to World/no-Scene; it now restores the author's last meaningful context (Global Nav tab, active Scene, `currentActivity`, `currentInspectorTarget`, and any open Frame ŌĆö covering SceneŌåÆHolderŌåÆFrame, SceneŌåÆText, SceneŌåÆDecorations chains) via a new `_loadEditingContext`/`_saveEditingContext` pair, hooked into the one function (`_renderWorkspace()`) every nav/selection change already calls, so no call site needed individual instrumentation. No architectural constraint blocked this ŌĆö the same `ProjectModel` lookups Working View already uses to render each state are enough to validate a remembered Scene/Holder/Layer/Frame still exists, falling back cleanly to World/no-Scene if one was deleted since. Deliberately stored under its own `vihu-world-builder-editing-context` localStorage key, never touching `project.updatedAt`/`ProjectStore.save` ŌĆö see (4). **(2) Explicit inactive states**: `_renderPreview()` previously always built a legacy Engine V1 specimen (from whichever Representation/Layout/Frame happened to be selected) into Working View and, when no Scene was active, into Runtime Preview too ŌĆö a pseudo-preview of World metadata Museum Theme authoring doesn't use. New `_renderInactiveWorkspace()` replaces both with an honest message whenever `!_activeSceneForRuntimePreview()` (nav-independent, matching AV-005's own "project-scoped" Runtime Preview rule) and nav isn't `'scenes'` (which already had its own equivalent Scene-Library empty state): Working View shows "No Scene yet. Create your first Scene to begin authoring." + a **+ Create Scene** button that jumps straight to the Scenes template picker when the World truly has zero Scenes (Blank World template, or before this session's ProjectModel.scenes() check returns empty), or the milder "No Scene open. Select a Scene to begin authoring." + **Go to Scenes** when Scenes exist but none is open (the common case, since every non-Blank template seeds one starter Scene ŌĆö so even a "brand-new" World already has a Scene, just not one currently selected); Runtime Preview shows the matching "Runtime Preview becomes available once a Scene has been created/is open." A real DOM bug surfaced building this: mounting the panel inside `.wb-working-canvas-inner` (the aspect-ratio-locked box) left it invisible, since that box collapses to near-zero size once its only normally-sized content ŌĆö the canvas ŌĆö is hidden; fixed by mounting on the outer `.wb-working-canvas-wrap` instead (a real flex:1 box, sized independent of canvas state) and explicitly hiding/showing the inner box alongside every other Working View state transition (identity card, Scene editor, Scene Library). **(3) Obvious route back to the Gallery**: a working `#wb-workspace-home` button already existed, but as a bare ­¤ÅĀ glyph with no visible text it was easy to mistake for a decorative brand mark rather than a navigation control (a real, disclosed UX gap, not a missing mechanism) ŌĆö it now reads "­¤ÅĀ My Worlds" with a bordered button treatment matching the header's other controls. **(4) Project Activity investigation**: extensive testing (immediate edits, drag-completions, full page reloads, multi-project scenarios) found `_persist()`/`ProjectStore.save()` and `renderMyWorlds()`'s fresh `ProjectStore.list()` read on every `showWelcome()` call both already work correctly ŌĆö no reproducible stale-timestamp bug was found in the current build. The one real risk this ticket's own "open time vs. edit time" hypothesis correctly anticipated is (1)'s new session-resume feature itself: had "remember where I was" been implemented by calling `ProjectStore.save()` on every navigation/selection change, merely *browsing* a World would have bumped `updatedAt` and made "Edited X ago" lie. Built defensively from the start via the separate `EDITING_CONTEXT_KEY` store instead, so navigation memory can never be mistaken for a content edit, now or in any future extension of it. Verified via Playwright: a brand-new Blank World shows the exact "No Scene yetŌĆ”"/"+ Create Scene" copy and the CTA opens the Scene Template picker directly; a template that seeds a starter Scene shows "No Scene openŌĆ”"/"Go to Scenes" instead; reopening a World resumes exactly on Manage Frames with the same Holder/Frame selected, and separately resumes on the same Text layer selected; deleting the remembered Scene and reopening falls back gracefully to World with zero console errors; the home button is clearly labelled; `updatedAt` still updates correctly on every save and survives reload. Full regression across every prior AV/AP/Slice/Validation/Build/Reorder/Project-Card suite passes unchanged; no Engine V2/Scene Model/rendering changes.)
- Authoring Validation AV-009 ŌĆö Hero Image silently failed to persist, root cause traced (not assumed) to a swallowed localStorage quota failure, not an Engine issue. **Root cause**: a realistic camera-resolution photo's data URL routinely runs several megabytes; `ProjectStore._writeAll` wrapped its `localStorage.setItem` in a bare `try{}catch(e){}` that discarded a thrown `QuotaExceededError` with no signal anywhere ŌĆö `_persist()` still showed "All Changes Saved," so the failure was invisible until the very next reload, when the stale pre-upload project (the last write that *did* fit) silently loaded back. Confirmed empirically: uploading a 5.7MB test image threw `QuotaExceededError` on `setItem`, and `preview.png` was absent from `localStorage` immediately after the "successful" save. **Fix, two parts**: (1) large image uploads are now downscaled/re-compressed client-side (`_downscaleImageDataURL` in `worldBuilderApp.js`, wired into the one shared `_fileInputUpload` every asset-upload control already uses ŌĆö Thumbnail, Hero Image, and the Assets screen's per-slot uploader all get the fix uniformly) ŌĆö only files whose data URL exceeds 1.5MB are touched, resized to a 1600px longest edge and re-encoded as JPEG at 0.85 quality, falling back to the original bytes if the shrunk version somehow isn't smaller; anything already small (icons, small graphics) passes through byte-for-byte untouched. (2) `ProjectStore.save()`/`_writeAll` no longer lie: `_writeAll` now returns `{ok, error}` instead of swallowing the exception, `save()` returns `{project, ok, error}` (no existing caller read the old return value, so widening it broke nothing), and `worldBuilderApp.js`'s `_persist()`/manual Save button now show a real, non-auto-dismissing ­¤ö┤ "Save Failed ŌĆö try a smaller image" state instead of "All Changes Saved" whenever a write doesn't actually reach localStorage ŌĆö a defensive backstop for any future asset that still doesn't fit, so a silent lie can never recur. Neither change touches Engine V2, the Scene Model, or any rendering path ŌĆö this is entirely `js/projectStore.js` and the Builder's own upload plumbing. Verified via Playwright end-to-end: upload a 5.7MB test photo as Hero Image ŌåÆ `localStorage` write succeeds (down from ~7.7MB base64 to ~1.8MB) with zero `setItem` errors ŌåÆ explicit Save ŌåÆ full page reload ŌåÆ reopen the World ŌåÆ Hero Image field shows the restored image ŌåÆ Project card (with a Thumbnail also uploaded) continues showing it ŌåÆ the empty Holder in a Scene renders the actual restored photo (pixel-sampled, not the generic placeholder colour) identically in Working View and Runtime Preview ŌåÆ Theme representation preview still renders. Full regression across every prior AV/AP/Slice/Validation/Build/Reorder/Project-Card suite passes unchanged; zero console errors; no Engine V2/Scene Model/rendering changes.)
- Authoring Validation AV-010 ŌĆö text editable bounds now auto-size to rendered width, not just height (a direct extension of AV-006, found continuing Museum Theme authoring: "New text" ŌåÆ "Big Tree" rendered correctly but the selection/drag box stayed at the full declared wrap-width). **Root cause**: AV-006's `textFootprint(ctx, layer, graph)` only ever measured height (line count ├Ś line height); it still returned the declared `rect.w`/`rect.x` untouched, so a short line of text kept the old, much-wider invisible box regardless of content. **Fix**: `textFootprint` now also measures the widest wrapped line via `ctx.measureText` and returns that as `w` (capped at the declared wrap width, since wrapping still can't render wider than its own container), with `x` offset per `align` exactly as `_paintLayer` computes `tx` (`left`ŌåÆ`rect.x`, `center`ŌåÆcentred within `rect.w`, `right`ŌåÆflush with `rect.x+rect.w`) ŌĆö reusing the same `_wrapLines` call so it can never drift from the real paint, matching AV-006's own one-source-of-truth pattern. `worldBuilderApp.js`'s drag-clamp now clamps `position.x` too (previously only `position.y`): since the footprint's x-offset from the declared box's own left edge is content/alignment-dependent but position-independent, it's computed once from the object's current position and reused to convert the footprint clamp back into a `position.x` clamp, correct for left/center/right alignment alike. Hit-testing and the selection outline already read `textFootprint` directly (AV-006), so both automatically inherit the width fix with no separate change. Only an explicit fixed-width text container (a capability this Builder hasn't built) would need to keep the declared box's width ŌĆö by default every text Layer now auto-sizes to its content, per this ticket's own product principle. Verified via Playwright: "Big Tree" (short, left-aligned) measures a footprint ~0.155 of canvas width vs. the declared 0.7 ŌĆö over 4├Ś narrower, matching the selection outline visibly hugging the glyphs; dragging the object now reaches xŌēł0.845 toward the right edge (previously capped near 0.3 by the old wide box). One prior AV-006 test needed its own click-target x-coordinate corrected (it assumed the old, incorrectly-wide hit area) ŌĆö not a regression, the exact intended consequence of this fix; re-verified AV-006's own original height-based scenario still passes unchanged. Full regression across every prior suite passes unchanged; zero console errors; Runtime rendering (`render()`/`_paintLayer`) byte-for-byte unchanged ŌĆö only an additive, non-drawing query function was extended, no Engine V2/Scene Model change.)
- Authoring Validation AV-011 ŌĆö rich text emoji authoring, via the existing EmojiPicker rather than a second picker (Museum Theme authoring needed decorative inline symbols ŌĆö "The Big Tree ­¤ī│," "By Vihaan ­¤¦Æ" ŌĆö with no convenient way to insert them). **Investigation**: `js/emojiPicker.js` already exists and is already wired onto every Text Element field in the main Studio app (Sprint 9.6) ŌĆö a small, self-contained module (`EmojiPicker.wrap(el)`) that wraps an existing `<input>`/`<textarea>` with a toggle button + emoji grid, inserting at the cursor and dispatching a real `input` event on the same element so it persists through whatever save path the field already had, with zero knowledge of the caller's own state. This is exactly "the simplest solution that provides a smooth authoring experience" the ticket asked for, so no new picker was built. **Implementation**: World Builder's `index.html` now loads `js/emojiPicker.js` alongside the other reused Studio Runtime scripts; `world-builder.css` gained the same `.emoji-picker-*` rules the main app's `css/style.css` already has, ported to Builder's own `--wb-*` variables (`--wb-border`/`--wb-cream`/`--wb-gold`/`--wb-paper`/`--wb-shadow`/`--wb-sand`) so the toggle/panel match Builder's theme rather than the main app's; `worldBuilderApp.js`'s Text Layer panel wraps its existing "Words" `_textarea(...)` with `EmojiPicker.wrap(...)` before mounting it in the field group ŌĆö no change to the textarea's own `input` handler, since EmojiPicker drives it through the identical event path a real keystroke would. Canvas `fillText` already renders emoji glyphs natively (a font/rendering-engine concern, not something Engine V2 needed to do anything for), so Working View and Runtime Preview show them identically with no renderer change. Verified via Playwright end-to-end: the ­¤śŖ toggle appears on the Words field, opens a 40-emoji grid, inserting one appends it into the textarea and immediately persists to the Scene Layer's `text`; both canvases render it identically; a full page reload and Scene reopen (AV-008's resume-context) shows the emoji-bearing text intact; a built Scene Package (Engine V2 Build) contains the emoji correctly UTF-8-encoded in its JSON. Full regression across every prior suite passes unchanged; zero console errors; no Engine V2/Scene Model/rendering changes ŌĆö the module is a Builder-only UI affordance reused as-is.)
- Builder V3 Experience Studio ŌĆö Milestone 1: Foundation terminology, Holder renamed to Place (per `docs/BUILDER_V3_EXPERIENCE_STUDIO.md`'s frozen Canon Decisions and the "Foundation (Final)" implementation-kickoff instruction: Foundation is `World ŌåÆ Scene ŌåÆ Place(s)`, a Builder authoring-language change only, explicitly not a new Engine ownership tier ŌĆö "internally, Engine V2 may continue using the existing Holder implementation if appropriate"). Scoped precisely to Engine V2's Scene Editor Place activity in `tools/world-builder/js/worldBuilderApp.js`/`js/projectModel.js`: every Builder-facing string a Theme Author sees (`_renderPlacePanel`'s heading/intro/empty-state/Add button, `_renderHolderPanel`'s "Place Name" field/Padding help text/Remove-and-back buttons, the Scene Header's Place count, the Place Boundary construction guide label) now says Place; the two data-level default names a new Holder is seeded with (`_holdersFor` for a fresh Scene Template, `addHolder` for one added later) changed from `'Holder'`/`'Holder N'` to `'Place'`/`'Place N'`, since those defaults are themselves user-visible text until a Theme Author renames one. Internal identifiers ŌĆö `holder`, `findHolder`/`updateHolder`/`addHolder`/`deleteHolder`, `scene.holders`, `holder.frame`/`.position`/`.size` ŌĆö are deliberately unchanged, exactly as the instruction permits, since renaming them would be pure internal churn with no Theme-Author-visible benefit and higher regression risk across a 4700-line file. First of several incremental, independently-verified milestones toward the full Experience Studio ŌĆö Experience data model, Nursery/Gallery, Experience Home navigation, the Inspector, and the Graduation workflow follow in subsequent commits, per the implementation brief's own "many small validated commits over one large rewrite" instruction.)
- Builder V3 Experience Studio ŌĆö Milestone 2: Experience Foundation + Experience Home (Parts 1-5 of `docs/BUILDER_V3_EXPERIENCE_STUDIO.md`'s implementation kickoff; explicitly architectural ŌĆö establishes the foundation every later milestone builds on, not a finished authoring experience). **Part 1 ŌĆö data model**: new `js/services/experienceSchema.js` holds a Builder-only, open `EXPERIENCE_TYPES` vocabulary (Frame/Decoration/Atmosphere/Lighting/Text Style) deliberately separate from `engineSchema.js`, since Experience is explicitly not an Engine V2 Canon concept; `js/projectModel.js` gained `experiences`/`findExperience`/`setExperience`/`addExperience`/`updateExperience`/`deleteExperience`/`validateExperiences`, persisted as `experiences/<id>.json` + a lazily-reconciled `experienceOrder` following the exact `_ordered` pattern `frameOrder`/`sceneOrder` already use, plus a `_ensureExperienceDefaults` read-time migration hook so a project saved before Experiences existed never crashes. Every Experience is created Nurturing; `deleteExperience` refuses anything else (Canon Decision #9 ŌĆö Delete exists only for Nurturing Experiences), enforced at this one choke point rather than left to the UI. `validateExperiences` is a plain, standalone hook ŌĆö not yet wired into the Validation screen (Milestone 3's own "Validation UX changes" scope) ŌĆö that skips Nurturing Experiences entirely, since they aren't part of the Theme yet. **Part 2 ŌĆö Global Navigation**: `Experiences` (­¤ī¤) becomes a permanent destination between Scenes and Validation. **Part 3 ŌĆö Experience Home**: a new `_renderExperiencesPanel` with two creative spaces, both reusing the proven `.wb-scene-library-grid`/`.wb-scene-card` visual language rather than inventing a second card system ŌĆö **The Gallery** ("what can I use today?", Theme Experiences only) and **The Nursery** ("what am I still growing?", Nurturing ideas only, never mixed with the Gallery per Canon Decisions #4/#5); Working View shows the same generic World-identity card already used for an empty Overview, since Experience Home has no single rendered page of its own to show there. **Part 4 ŌĆö Experience Cards**: domain-sensitive ŌĆö a Gallery card shows preview/name/description/type/attachment/ownership(lifecycle)/usage/tags; a Nursery card deliberately omits ownership and usage, since neither concept exists yet for an unpromoted idea (usage is hardcoded to "Used by 0 Hosts" in the Gallery this milestone, since nothing can attach until Milestone 3). **Part 5 ŌĆö placeholder creation**: a minimal inline form (Name/Type/Intended Attachment/Description) reachable only from the Nursery's "+ New Experience," saving via `addExperience` and always landing Nurturing ŌĆö no Inspector, no Graduation, no attach-to-Place/Scene, no Reuse Existing, no Usage Explorer, all explicitly out of this milestone's scope per its own brief. Verified via Playwright end-to-end: the Gallery's honest empty state (with a direct "Go to the Nursery" bridge, never a dead end) and the Nursery's own empty state; creating "Wax Seal" (Decoration, Free) and seeing it appear immediately with the correct Nursery-omitted fields; a full page reload and Scene-list reopen showing the Experience intact; Delete removing it correctly. Full regression across `goldenBuild.js` (30/30) and the AV-001/AV-003/AV-006/runtime/validation/build/reorder/place-rename suites all pass unchanged; zero unexpected console errors; no Engine V2/Runtime/rendering change ŌĆö this milestone is entirely new, additive Builder data and UI, with Frame/Decoration/Text's existing authoring paths completely untouched.)
- Builder V3 Experience Studio ŌĆö Milestone 3: Experience Authoring (completes the Creative Journey from `docs/BUILDER_V3_EXPERIENCE_STUDIO.md`: Inspector, Graduation, Ownership, Attachment, Contextual Authoring, Usage Explorer, Reuse Existing, and Validation integration, all built and Playwright-verified together). **Terminology review**: Milestone 1/2's own retrospective found "draft" still describing World Projects while Experiences already said Nurturing ŌĆö `js/projectStore.js`'s two status-assignment sites now write `'growing'`, with a defensive read-time fallback in `worldBuilderApp.js` so an already-saved `'draft'` project displays correctly with no migration write; `templates.js`'s unrelated "Drafts"/"draft" tags on the Sketchbook template (describing the *kind* of artwork, not Builder's own lifecycle concept) are deliberately left alone. **Data model** (`js/projectModel.js`): `graduateToPersonal(project, id, sceneId)`/`graduateToPublic(project, id)` implement the frozen fork ŌĆö Nurturing goes directly to Personal (recording which Scene) or straight to Public; Personal may later choose Public; there is no reverse path, enforced at the model layer, not just the UI. Milestone 2's placeholder singular `host` field is replaced by a real `attachments` array (a Public Experience may attach to many Hosts at once) ŌĆö a safe, lossless migration since Milestone 2 shipped no attachment workflow at all, so every existing `host` was already null. `attachExperience`/`detachExperience` enforce real ownership rules (Nurturing can never attach; Personal may only attach within its own `scopeSceneId`) and validate the target Scene/Place actually exists; `usageOf` resolves every attachment to real Scene/Place names for the Usage Explorer. **The mirroring bridge** (`_syncExperienceAttachments`) is a compatibility shortcut into Engine V2's existing, unmodified rendering mechanisms ŌĆö never a change to `engineRuntime.js` or the Scene Model. Investigation found only two real projection targets exist today: a Place's single Frame slot (Engine Canon ┬¦9) and a Scene's Layer array (Engine Canon ┬¦7) ŌĆö there is no Holder Layer mechanism yet for anything else to attach to a Place (Scene Model ┬¦7, still an open question, not resolved here). This is disclosed honestly rather than papered over: `js/services/experienceSchema.js`'s `EXPERIENCE_TYPES` now carries a `renders: {attached, free}` flag per type ŌĆö Frame mirrors into the Place's `frame` field when Attached; Decoration/Text mirror into a Scene Layer (tagged with a new, additive `sourceExperienceId` back-reference) when Free; Atmosphere/Lighting/Text Style record real attachments (Usage still works) but paint nothing yet, since Engine V2 has no rendering concept for them at any granularity ŌĆö the Inspector shows an honest inline note whenever a chosen type+attachment combination has no render path. Also found and corrected: the approved Experience Types vocabulary (Frame/Decoration/Atmosphere/Lighting/Text Style) had no type for actual text *content* (only "Text Style," which is styling-only) ŌĆö Museum Theme's real Museum Caption need requires one, so a "Text" type was added, additively, alongside Text Style rather than overloading it. `validateExperiences` extended: every attachment must reference a real Scene/Place; a Personal Experience's attachments must stay within its own `scopeSceneId`. **Experience Inspector**: clicking any card (Gallery or Nursery) selects it and replaces the grid with its Inspector, exactly like selecting a Place already does ŌĆö no dedicated Experience workspace (Blueprint ┬¦6.1's philosophy, restated). Properties render per Type, mirroring the exact field shape the existing Frame/Decoration/Text authoring surfaces already use, so editing here and editing the old surface never disagree about what a field means; every edit re-syncs any live attachment immediately. Ownership renders the frozen fork (Graduate to Personal/Public side by side while Nurturing; only Make Public while Personal; neither while Public) with no reverse-path action anywhere in the UI. Usage Explorer lists every real attachment, each entry doubling as one-click Detach; the Attach control is the same one mechanism for "attach somewhere new" and "Reuse Existing" browsed from the Gallery. **Contextual authoring** (Place's Frame picker, Decorations'/Text's no-selection states): an "Experiences" block offers "+ Add Experience" (creates Nurturing, then immediately graduates to Personal scoped to this Scene and attaches in one motion ŌĆö a disclosed convenience, since a Theme Author clicking this wants it here, now, not a trip to the Nursery) and "Reuse Existing Experience" (browses already-Public, type-compatible Experiences and attaches directly); once attached, the block shows "Attached: `<name>`" with a one-click "Open in Experience Home ŌåÆ" ŌĆö the old Frame/Decoration/Text authoring stays fully functional alongside this (no destructive migration), giving both paths side by side while Experience-first authoring becomes preferred. **Validation**: a new "Experiences" section mirrors the existing "Scenes (Engine V2)" pattern exactly ŌĆö its own separate report, run alongside the other two, Nursery items excluded entirely. Verified end-to-end via Playwright across every piece: Nurturing cannot attach; graduation requires and records a Scene for Personal; attaching a Frame Experience sets the Place's real frame reference and creates a correctly-synced mirrored Frame record, visible immediately in both Working View and Runtime Preview; a Personal Experience is correctly refused attachment outside its own Scene; a Decoration/Text Experience attach creates a correctly-tagged mirrored Scene Layer; a full Museum Theme walkthrough (a Frame Experience reused across two Places in a "Gallery Wall," a Text Experience for a Museum Caption, a Decoration Experience for a Wax Seal, all created via contextual authoring) produces a clean Validation report with zero console errors; a Milestone-2-era project record (pre-`attachments`, `host: null`) loads and migrates correctly with no crash, confirming existing projects keep working. Full regression across `goldenBuild.js` (30/30) and every prior AV/runtime/validation/build/reorder/place-rename/experience-home suite passes unchanged. No Engine V2/Runtime/Story Studio change; no Builder navigation redesign; no new product concepts beyond what the frozen design already specified.)
- Builder V3 Experience Studio ŌĆö Canon Alignment Sprint / Product Model Purification (a deliberate pause on Experience feature work, run immediately after Milestone 3, to align implementation with the approved paper design rather than add capability ŌĆö "the objective is not more capability, the objective is conceptual clarity," per the sprint's own closing instruction; produced `docs/BUILDER_V3_CANON_ALIGNMENT_REPORT.md`, the permanent four-section checkpoint (Confirmed Product Concepts / Engine Adapter Concepts / Resolved Inconsistencies / Open Questions) this entry summarizes). **Hosted By replaces Attachment**: the binary Attached/Free axis (`js/services/experienceSchema.js`'s `EXPERIENCE_ATTACHMENTS`, `js/projectModel.js`'s `exp.attachment`) is replaced by the frozen three-way product model ŌĆö Place / Scene / Free (`EXPERIENCE_HOSTS`, `exp.hostedBy`) ŌĆö because Milestone 3's binary model had no way to express "fills the whole Scene" (e.g. a full-bleed background), a real product-model gap surfaced by implementation, not a bug; the migration is lossless (`_ensureExperienceDefaults`: old `'attached'` ŌåÆ `'place'`, everything else ŌåÆ `'free'`). "Hosted by Scene" is wired to the pre-existing full-bleed background fill mechanism (`setSceneBackground`) rather than any new Engine capability ŌĆö `decoration` is the one Experience Type whose `renders` map gained a real `scene: true`, since its existing `color` property is exactly what that fill needs. Every author-facing string was updated to match (Card meta line via a new shared `_hostedByLabel` helper, Inspector heading, the renamed Host/Reuse picker ŌĆö "Attach"/"Attach Here" ŌåÆ "Host Here" ŌĆö the contextual "Attached: `<name>`" note ŌåÆ "Hosting: `<name>`", and the Nursery quick-create form's "Intended Attachment" field ŌåÆ "Hosted By"); the internal `exp.attachments` array (real usage/placement records) was deliberately left unrenamed, since it's never shown to an author as a raw field name and renaming it would be pure internal churn the sprint's own "remove leakage, not capability" framing argues against. **Engine Adapter boundary made explicit** (Objective 5's "Experience Ōåō Frame Ōåō Scene Layer Ōåō Runtime" chain): `projectModel.js`'s `_syncExperienceAttachments` is now doc-comment-labeled as *the* Engine Adapter ŌĆö the one function allowed to know a Place-hosted Frame projects onto a Place's `frame` slot, a Scene-hosted Experience onto the background fill Layer, and a Free-hosted Decoration/Text onto a tagged Scene Layer; nothing else in the Inspector/Card/picker code touches this translation. `experienceSchema.js`'s `renders` map (now `{place, scene, free}` per Type, renamed from `rendersWhenAttached` to `rendersWhenHosted`) is documented as Engine Adapter *metadata riding on* a product field ŌĆö it discloses what the current adapter can paint, but Hosted By itself stays a pure product choice regardless. Two literal author-facing "Engine V2" wording leaks (the Inspector's two disclosure notes in `_renderExperienceProperties`) were found via a full audit and rewritten in plain product language ("doesn't appear on the page yet ŌĆö that's coming in a future Builder release"); every other "Engine V2" occurrence in the codebase was confirmed to be a code comment, never rendered UI text, and left alone, since the mandate was about what an author sees. **Type field reviewed, not restructured** (Objective 3): confirmed the field currently serves two purposes at once ŌĆö a legitimate creative decision (which Properties fields the Inspector shows) and an Engine Adapter dispatch key (which mirror routine runs) ŌĆö documented as an Open Question rather than split into two fields, since doing so would be new data-model capability, out of this sprint's paused scope. **Experience ŌåÆ Objects deferred** (Objective 4): confirmed today's one-implicit-shape-per-Type design is not a prohibited "specialized subclass," but is also not yet the frozen model's `objects[]` array; building that this sprint would have been new capability, so it's recorded as an Open Question instead. Atmosphere/Lighting/Text Style (zero adapter, zero Museum Theme usage) were kept per "do not remove capabilities" and disclosed honestly as reserved vocabulary, also an Open Question. `docs/BUILDER_V3_EXPERIENCE_STUDIO.md` gained a new Part 2.1 (Canon Alignment Addendum) with a translation table for reading every earlier Part's "Attachment" language as "Hosted By," plus a v1.2 Change History entry ŌĆö chosen deliberately over silently rewriting all 19 "Attachment" occurrences scattered through the document's prose, so the terminology change is traceable rather than silently reinterpreted. Verified via Playwright: Place/Scene/Free hosting all round-trip correctly (a Place-hosted Frame still sets the real `holder.frame` reference; a Scene-hosted Decoration correctly sets the Scene's background color; a Free-hosted Text still mirrors to a tagged Scene Layer); the Inspector and Gallery/Nursery cards show zero "Attached"/"Attachment" wording and correct "Hosted by X" copy throughout; a Milestone-2-era legacy record (`attachment: 'free'`) migrates correctly to `hostedBy: 'free'` with no crash; full regression across `goldenBuild.js` (30/30) and every prior Milestone 2/3/AV/AP/runtime/validation/build/reorder/place-rename suite passes unchanged (one test script, `wb_m3_inspector_test.js`, was itself updated for the intentional `'attached'` ŌåÆ `'place'` enum rename ŌĆö not a product regression). No Engine V2/Scene Model/Runtime change; no new Experience capability added, per this sprint's own "pause feature development" instruction.)
- Builder V3 MEP ŌĆö Experience Builder Foundation (the first Builder MEP implementation milestone, explicitly scoped down twice during planning to stay additive: no Experience persistence redesign, no Parts array, no data migration, no Type field removal, no new Builder concepts such as Recipes ŌĆö "reuse the existing implementation wherever possible," per the approved plan's own governing rule, "can the Museum Theme be authored more naturally after this change?"). **Host-aware Bounds** (new Builder Canon rule ŌĆö the Host determines the bounds): the Experience Inspector gained a "Bounds" section, inserted right after Properties ŌĆö Hosted by Scene shows a static "Inherited from Scene (read-only)" note, Hosted by Place shows "Inherited from Place (read-only)," and only Hosted by Free shows real, editable X %/Y %/Width %/Height % sliders; those Free sliders read and write the *same* mirrored Scene Layer's existing `position`/`size` that Working View has always dragged (AV-006/AV-010) ŌĆö a second, synced entry point onto data that already existed, never a duplicate store. `js/projectModel.js` gained exactly one small, additive export, `findMirroredSceneLayer` (exposing the pre-existing private `_findMirroredLayer` lookup rather than duplicating it), and a new `_experienceFreeLayer(exp)` helper in `worldBuilderApp.js` resolves an Experience's first Free usage entry to its real mirrored Layer via that export + the existing `findSceneLayer` (for defaults reconciliation). **Decoration Image**: an optional `image` property (a data URI) sits alongside Decoration's existing `glyph`/`color` in the same flat `properties` bag ŌĆö per explicit instruction, Image and Glyph are deliberately *not* mutually exclusive in the underlying model (both are simply optional properties, "permissive for future evolution"), only in which one the Runtime prefers when painting. The Experience Properties panel's Decoration branch gained one field reusing `_assetUploadRow`/`_fileInputUpload` verbatim ŌĆö the exact same controls Overview's Thumbnail/Hero Image fields already use ŌĆö no new upload infrastructure of any kind. **Runtime** (`js/services/engineRuntime.js`): `_paintLayer`'s decoration branch is extended, not rewritten ŌĆö it now checks for a loaded Image first, via a new optional `resolveLayerImage` callback threaded onto `load()`'s 4th parameter (mirroring the existing `resolveFrame`/`representativeImage` "caller resolves, this module only draws" pattern exactly, so the module stays pure and synchronous), and falls back to the pre-existing glyph `fillText` when none is available or not yet decoded. `worldBuilderApp.js` gained a small, generic image cache (`_resolveLayerImage`/`_layerImageCache`), the identical async-decode-then-redraw shape EV-002's `_representativeArtworkImage` already established for the one Holder-artwork slot, now generalized to any Scene Layer's `image` field. Type is deliberately unchanged and unremoved throughout ŌĆö every Experience still carries a `type`, still read internally by the Engine Adapter for dispatch, exactly as before this milestone; "Parts" (Color/Border/Image/Text) stayed a conceptual label only, never a stored array. Verified via Playwright: Place-hosted and Scene-hosted Experiences show the correct read-only Bounds note with zero editable fields; a Free-hosted Text Experience shows all four editable bounds fields and a Width % drag correctly writes the real mirrored Layer's `size.w` (confirmed via direct model inspection); a Decoration Experience's Image field uploads correctly, sets `properties.image` without clearing `properties.glyph`, and the Runtime visibly prefers the uploaded Image over the glyph in both Working View and Runtime Preview (pixel-sampled against the exact known decoded color of the test fixture); full regression across `goldenBuild.js` (30/30) and every prior Milestone/Canon-Alignment/AV/AP/runtime/validation/build/reorder/place-rename suite passes unchanged; zero console errors. No Engine V2/Scene Model redesign; no Parts persistence; no migration; no Type removal; no new Builder concepts.)
- Builder V3 MEP ŌĆö Museum Authoring Complete (the second Builder MEP implementation milestone, driven by a hands-on authoring pass ŌĆö building the actual Museum Theme through the Builder exactly as a Theme Author would, rather than a feature-by-feature review ŌĆö per the milestone's own "does this help an author build the Museum Theme?" test. Every fix below is additive/corrective; no new Builder concepts, no architecture change. **(1) Starter Scene name/shape mismatch**: the Artwork Gallery template's seeded Scene was named "Showcase" ("big and bold, the classic gallery look") but defaulted to Portrait, since its Engine Scene Template (`single-holder`) always does; `TEMPLATE_STARTER_SCENE` gained an optional `aspect` override applied via the existing `setSceneAspect` right after seeding ŌĆö Showcase now seeds Landscape. **(2) Legacy Frame picker/Usage desync ŌĆö a real correctness bug**: the Place panel's pre-Experience "FRAME" picker (kept functional since Milestone 3's "both paths side by side" decision) wrote `holder.frame` directly via `updateHolder`, bypassing `attachExperience`/`detachExperience` ŌĆö switching or clearing a Place's Frame through that picker left a hosting Experience's `attachments` record stale, so Usage/Gallery bookkeeping silently lied about where an Experience was actually hosted. Fixed by making `_setHolderFrame` Experience-aware: detaches any currently-hosting Frame Experience properly before applying a new selection, attaches through the real mechanism when the newly-picked Frame is itself Experience-backed. **(3) Decorations list leaked Text layers**: `_renderDecorationsPanel`'s existing-items filter was `kind !== 'fill'` instead of `kind === 'decoration'`, so Text layers appeared misfiled inside the Decorations activity; fixed, and the card icon now shows an uploaded Image (Prompt 1's Decoration Image support) instead of only ever reading `.glyph`. **(4) New Decorations/Text spawned dead-center**: `addSceneLayer`'s default `position` was `{0.4, 0.4}` ŌĆö directly on top of a Scene's usual Place ŌĆö so a freshly-created Free Experience was often invisible or accidentally selected instead of the artwork right after creation; moved to `{0.38, 0.82}` (clear of a typical Place, still exactly as draggable), fixed at both call sites (the default itself, and the standalone "Add a Decoration" glyph-picker's hardcoded duplicate) ŌĆö this also serendipitously improved the Experience-based Text creation path's default position to better match a real Museum Caption's actual below-the-photo placement. **(5) Inspector field grouping**: the Experience Properties panel was the one Inspector still stacking every field full-width; paired via the existing `_fieldRow`/`_buildFieldGroup` convention Frames/Layouts/Overview already use (Mat Width|Frame Thickness, Border Colour|Wall Tone for Frame; Glyph|Colour for Decoration; Font|Alignment, Font Size|Colour for Text/Text Style). **(6) Usage completeness**: nothing told an author that editing a reused Public Experience silently changes every place it's hosted; `_renderExperienceProperties` now shows "Editing this updates everywhere it's hosted ŌĆö N places right now" whenever real usage exceeds one, reading the same `usageOf` data "Used In" already lists. **(7) Gallery card previews**: every card showed the same generic Type icon regardless of content, so several Frame variations or Decorations were indistinguishable at a glance; a Frame card now shows its real border-colour swatch (same style the legacy Frame picker uses) and a Decoration card shows its real Image or Glyph. **Considered and deliberately declined**: fast-pathing "Hosted by Scene" creation from the Decorations panel's contextual quick-create ŌĆö the panel's own pre-existing dedicated Background colour field already fully covers the real per-Scene wall-colour need with zero ceremony, and Scene-hosted Experiences remain reachable via the Nursery's full form plus Reuse for the rarer cross-Scene-consistency case; adding a Hosted-By selector to the fast quick-create form would cut against "smooth creation flow" for no Museum-Theme-blocking gain. Verified via a new consolidated Playwright regression covering all seven fixes plus a full end-to-end Museum Theme authoring pass (Scene ŌåÆ Place ŌåÆ Frame Experience ŌåÆ Text Experience ŌåÆ Decoration Experience ŌåÆ cross-scene reuse ŌåÆ Usage Explorer ŌåÆ Gallery ŌåÆ Validation ŌåÆ Build ŌåÆ Publish, with a 900-sample pixel-parity check confirming zero difference between Working View and Runtime Preview); full regression across `goldenBuild.js` (30/30) and every prior Milestone/Canon-Alignment/MEP/AV/AP/runtime/validation/build/reorder/place-rename suite passes unchanged (one test's own hardcoded pixel-sample coordinates needed updating for the intentional spawn-position fix ŌĆö not a regression; one pre-existing timing-flaky test confirmed flaky on the unmodified baseline too via `git stash`, unrelated to this milestone). No Engine V2/Scene Model/Runtime redesign; every fix reuses existing mechanisms.)
- Builder V3 MEP Freeze ŌĆö Release Candidate Audit (the closing MEP milestone: "treat Builder V3 as if it is shipping tomorrow." Five audits, not another feature pass. **Audit 1 (fresh authoring pass) surfaced this milestone's most significant finding**: a systemic data-loss bug across all three Experience-backed legacy editing surfaces kept intentionally functional since Milestone 3 ("both paths side by side") ŌĆö the Text Layer panel, the Decoration Layer panel's Name field, and the "Manage Frames" screen all wrote directly to the mirrored Layer/Frame record (`updateSceneLayer`/`setFrameField`/`setFrameFieldValue`), bypassing the owning Experience's own `properties` entirely; since the Engine Adapter (`_mirrorSceneLayer`/`_mirrorFrame`) unconditionally re-derives the mirror from `properties` on every sync, the next unrelated Experience-Inspector edit silently discarded whatever had just been typed or changed through the legacy surface ŌĆö reproduced with real data (a typed Museum Caption's words vanishing after an unrelated Colour edit; a Manage-Frames Wall Tone change reverting after an unrelated Shadow edit). Fixed identically in all three places, mirroring the exact adapter-routing pattern the previous milestone already established for the legacy Frame picker: when Experience-backed, field writes route through `updateExperience`/`updateExperienceProperty` instead of the mirror directly. A related bug found in the same investigation: `_mirrorSceneLayer`'s `text`-branch sync omitted `color` entirely, so a Text Experience's Colour field persisted but silently never rendered ŌĆö fixed by adding it to the synced set. **Audit 2 (consistency sweep)** found the Canon Alignment Sprint's AttachmentŌåÆHosted-By rename had missed one button ("Create & Attach" ŌåÆ "Create & Host"), and normalized the Experience Inspector's delete button to "Delete this Experience" (matching Place/Decoration/Text's "Remove this X" convention while keeping the deliberately stronger "Delete" verb ŌĆö Canon Decision #9's one real, permanent deletion); confirmed zero "Engine V1"/"Engine V2"/"Scene Layer" in any literal UI string, and confirmed the one remaining "Holder" occurrence (`_renderLayoutsPanel`'s "Holder Area" diagram) is unreachable from any UI control in Builder V3 (no Global Navigation entry or bridge link since Slice 1) ŌĆö left as the pre-existing, already-documented dead code it is. **Audit 3 (Working View vs. Runtime pixel-level review)**: a full-canvas diff (not sampled) on a fully-authored Scene with nothing selected found 12,240 differing pixels out of 1,458,000, traced to a thin border-shaped pattern spanning 976 of 1,080 rows ŌĆö matching exactly the known, always-on Safe Area guide (Blueprint ┬¦7, Working-View-only by design), not any accidental content difference; confirmed intentional, left unchanged. **Audit 4 (Experience System workflow completeness)** verified creation/editing/hosting/reuse/graduation/deletion/validation/publishing all function correctly via the fixes above plus full regression. **Audit 5 (regression)**: full existing suite plus a new end-to-end proof ŌĆö authored a complete 3-Scene Museum Theme (Showcase/Portrait/Quote) with a Public Frame Experience reused across two Scenes, a Text Experience Museum Caption, a Decoration Experience Wax Seal, and a Scene-hosted Quote background ŌĆö reaching a clean Validation (0 errors, 0 warnings, every category), a successful Scene Package Build, a successful World Package Build, and a fully functional Publish screen. Full regression across `goldenBuild.js` (30/30) and every prior Milestone/Canon-Alignment/MEP/AV/AP/runtime/validation/build/reorder/place-rename suite passes unchanged. No Engine V2/Scene Model/Runtime redesign; no new Builder concepts; every fix reuses the exact adapter-routing pattern already established for the legacy Frame picker. Builder V3 MEP is frozen as of this milestone ŌĆö see the Final Deliverable report for the full MEP Status checklist, remaining-issues statement, deferred-ideas list, and release recommendation.)
- Builder V3.1 ŌĆö Universal Experience Authoring (removes the biggest remaining source of Museum Theme authoring friction found across the MEP milestones: the Experience Type picker, which forced an author to choose an implementation category ŌĆö Frame/Decoration/Text/Atmosphere/Lighting/Text Style ŌĆö before a creative idea even existed. **Type selector removed**: the Nursery's "+ New Experience" form no longer shows a Type field; every new Experience internally defaults to the existing Decoration implementation (`js/services/experienceSchema.js`'s `DEFAULT_EXPERIENCE_TYPE`) ŌĆö an Engine Adapter detail the author never sees; the Experience Card and Inspector header both dropped their Type label to match. **Universal content**: every Experience ŌĆö new or pre-existing ŌĆö now exposes the same four content sections in its Inspector, each with its own Properties and Transform (Move/Resize): ­¤ōØ Text (Content/Font/Size/Weight/Alignment/Colour/Opacity), ­¤¢╝ Image (Upload/Replace/Remove/Preview/Fit/Opacity), ­¤ÄŁ Graphics (a reusable SVG/PNG visual asset, no Fit control), and ­¤Ä© Colour (Colour Picker/Opacity/Transparent checkbox, so an Experience can be pure Text/Image/Graphics with no fill at all). Implemented additively ŌĆö `js/services/experienceSchema.js` gained `defaultUniversalContent()`, a set of entirely new namespaced property keys (`textContent`/`textFont`/`textSize`/`textWeight`/`textAlign`/`textColor`/`textOpacity`/`textX/Y/W/H`, the equivalent `image*`/`graphic*` sets, `colorValue`/`colorOpacity`/`colorTransparent`) merged into every type's `defaultProperties()`, deliberately distinct from every legacy field name so a pre-existing Frame's mat/border/wallTone/shadow fields and a pre-existing Decoration's/Text's legacy fields are never touched; `js/projectModel.js`'s `_ensureExperienceDefaults` gained a read-time `_ensureUniversalContentDefaults` migration (one-time per Experience) that seeds the new fields and copies a legacy Decoration's `image`ŌåÆ`imageSrc` / legacy Text's `text`/`font`/`fontSize`/`align`/`color`ŌåÆ`textContent`/`textFont`/`textSize`/`textAlign`/`textColor` ŌĆö a legacy Decoration's `color`ŌåÆ`colorValue` is copied but `colorTransparent` deliberately stays at its fresh default (`true`) rather than flipping to visible, since `color` was already inert on a Decoration Layer and flipping it live would have been an undisclosed visual regression, not a migration. **Engine Adapter extended, not replaced**: Scene-/Free-hosted Experiences now sync through a new `_syncUniversalContent` (Place-hosting stays Frame-only, a disclosed gap ŌĆö no Holder Layer stack exists yet for anything else to project onto) that mirrors up to four tagged Scene Layers per Experience, one per populated Text/Image/Graphics/Colour section, reusing the exact unmodified Layer kinds Engine V2 already renders (`fill` for Colour, `text` for Text, `decoration` with `.image` set for both Image and Graphics ŌĆö the same mechanism Builder V3 MEP's Decoration Image support already proved out); an empty section mirrors nothing. Colour has no Transform of its own ŌĆö its rect is the live bounding box of whichever Text/Image/Graphics is currently populated, recomputed on every sync. A pre-existing Experience's single untagged mirrored Layer is *claimed* in place (same position, re-tagged) the first time it's touched under the new model rather than orphaned while a duplicate is created at a default rect ŌĆö verified directly. The Free-hosted "Bounds" editor from Builder V3 MEP is superseded by each section's own Transform; the Inspector's Bounds section is now purely informational for all three Hosted-By values. `js/services/engineRuntime.js`'s `_paintLayer` gained a generic `layer.opacity` read (`ctx.globalAlpha`, defaulting to 1 so every pre-existing Layer renders byte-identically) and an `imageFit`-aware `layer.fit` read (defaulting to 'fit', matching prior hardcoded behaviour) ŌĆö both apply uniformly across Layer kinds, not as per-content-type special cases. **P0 image upload bug, root-caused not patched**: instrumented the full pipeline (upload ŌåÆ Asset ŌåÆ Experience property ŌåÆ Engine Adapter mirror ŌåÆ Working View ŌåÆ Runtime Preview) and found all six links already worked correctly; the actual defect was the Inspector's own upload row never re-rendering after a successful upload, so it visibly stayed on "Upload" with no thumbnail even though the upload had already fully succeeded everywhere else ŌĆö exactly what reads as "the button doesn't work" to an author watching the one place they're looking. Fixed with a narrowly-scoped `onUploadProp(key)` (used only by Image/Graphics upload rows, not every Properties field) that re-renders the panel after persisting; `_assetUploadRow` also gained a Remove action, a side effect also reaching Overview's pre-existing Thumbnail/Hero Image rows. Gallery/Nursery cards now prefer whichever universal section is populated (Image, then Graphics, then a non-transparent Colour) over the old Type-icon fallback for their thumbnail. Verified via Playwright end to end: no Type field anywhere in creation; all four sections present with working Transform for every Experience regardless of legacy type (a legacy Frame Experience keeps its own dedicated fields too, unchanged); an Image upload's row updates immediately and the uploaded pixels render identically in Working View and Runtime Preview; a Colour fill renders correctly at the live content footprint once positioned clear of the Place; Graphics Opacity blends visibly; a hand-constructed pre-V3.1 legacy Decoration Experience migrates correctly on read, keeps rendering from its original untouched Layer until first touched, then claims that same Layer in place with no duplication; a full Museum Theme authoring pass (Frame Experience, Text ŌåÆ Museum Caption via the universal Text section, Decoration ŌåÆ Wax Seal) reaches a clean Validation, successful Scene and World Package Builds, and a functional Publish screen. `goldenBuild.js` passes 30/30 unchanged; zero console errors. No Engine V2/Scene Model/Runtime redesign beyond the two small, generic `_paintLayer` additions; no persistence redesign; the Engine Adapter boundary remains the one place a Builder-facing Experience is projected onto Engine V2's own, otherwise-unmodified rendering mechanisms.)
- Working View Experience Studio (restores the Builder's original two-view philosophy ŌĆö Runtime Preview is always the Reader's complete published Scene, Working View is the Author's own isolated workspace ŌĆö which Universal Experience Authoring had inadvertently left broken: `_workingViewIsIdentityCard()` returned `true` for the entire Experiences nav unconditionally, so selecting any Experience from the Gallery or Nursery still showed the plain World identity card in Working View, never the Experience itself, while Runtime Preview correctly kept showing the active Scene throughout. **Root cause**: `_experienceCard`'s click handler and the Inspector's "ŌåÉ Back"/"Delete this Experience" buttons all only ever called `_renderContextPanel()` (repaints the Context Inspector alone) instead of `_renderWorkspace()` (which also calls `_renderPreview()`) ŌĆö Working View was structurally unreachable from Experience selection no matter how the isolated Studio itself was built; fixed at that exact source. **The isolated Studio**: a new `_renderExperienceStudio(exp)` crops Working View to just the selected Experience's own populated content ŌĆö `js/projectModel.js` exports the same rect math the Engine Adapter already uses for a Free-hosted Colour fill's footprint (`experienceContentFootprint`), padded 18% and normalized to a ~900px canvas, independent of the rest of the Scene (a Nurturing Experience with no Scene at all renders identically). Colour fills the whole isolated canvas or shows a real checkerboard when Transparent; Image, Graphics, and Text all paint via one new export, `EngineV2Runtime.paintLayer` ŌĆö the exact `_paintLayer` function `render()` already uses internally, reused directly rather than reimplemented. Each populated section gets a selection outline + resize handle (reusing the Scene editor's own `_drawSelectionOutline`) ŌĆö Move and Resize for Text/Image/Graphics alike, a deliberately expanded affordance specific to this new isolated Studio (the Scene editor's own Working View and its reposition-only Decorations/Text convention are untouched). **Move/Resize dragging** is a second click-to-drag driver (`_experienceStudioDragState`), separate from the Scene editor's own `_holderDragState`, writing the dragged section's X/Y or W/H directly via `updateExperienceProperty` on every mousemove tick (verified live-syncing Runtime Preview ŌĆö a moved image's pixels appear at their new location mid-drag, before mouseup) while redrawing the Studio against the same frozen stage/canvas size the gesture started with, never recomputing a fresh crop mid-drag (which would otherwise chase its own tail, since the very rect being dragged is part of what decides the crop) ŌĆö the stage only re-settles to a fresh fit on mouseup, mirroring the Scene editor's own established freeze/mutate/persist shape exactly. Verified end to end via Playwright: selecting an Experience shows a small, correctly-cropped isolated canvas distinct from the full Scene's own dimensions while Runtime Preview keeps showing the complete Scene unchanged; Colour Transparent shows a real checkerboard; Image/Graphics uploads render immediately; dragging an uploaded Image moves it with Runtime Preview reflecting the new position mid-drag; "ŌåÉ Back" correctly restores the identity card; the Scene editor's own Working View is completely unaffected. Full regression across `goldenBuild.js` (30/30) and every V3.1 verification script passes unchanged; zero console errors. No Engine V2/Scene Model/Runtime redesign; no new product concepts; Working View is the permanent Experience authoring workspace going forward.)
- Authoring Convergence Sprint (a pause-on-features, converge-toward-one-pipeline sprint ŌĆö the Builder had two enrichment authoring systems, legacy Place/Decoration/Text ŌåÆ Scene Layer ŌåÆ Runtime and Experience ŌåÆ Engine Adapter ŌåÆ Runtime, and this sprint began closing that gap rather than widening it. **The two concrete parallel-creation paths converged**: the Decorations panel's glyph-picker grid and the Text panel's "Ō×Ģ Add Text" button both used to call `addSceneLayer` directly, producing a plain Scene Layer with no Experience behind it. Both now call the same `addExperience` ŌåÆ `graduateToPersonal` ŌåÆ `attachExperience` sequence "+ Add Experience" already uses, landing on the new Experience's own Inspector immediately ŌĆö a picked glyph is rasterized into a small PNG (`_rasterizeGlyphToDataURL`) stored as the Experience's Graphics section content (the Universal content model has no bare glyph concept of its own); "Add Text" seeds the Text section's `textContent` directly. **Runtime consistency**: a new `_experienceHostingStatus(exp)` compares an Experience's real Usage against the currently open Scene and shows a plain banner in the isolated Experience Studio whenever Working View and Runtime Preview would otherwise silently disagree ("Not yet hosted anywhereŌĆ”" / "Hosted in `<Scene>` ŌĆö open that Scene to see it in Runtime Preview"), nothing when they already match ŌĆö a synchronization-status readout over existing `usageOf` data, not a new renderer. **Host Here redundancy fixed**: a Personal Experience scoped to one Scene and already hosted there now shows "Already hosted in `<Scene>` ŌĆö nothing more to host here" instead of a redundant picker; otherwise the "Host Here" button recomputes live as the Scene/Place dropdowns change, reading "Ō£ō Already Hosted Here" (disabled) once the selection matches a real Usage entry. **A disclosed, deliberately-deferred exception**: Frame's dual identity (a reusable Theme Asset shelf in its own right, and something an Experience can front-end) was investigated and left untouched ŌĆö the sprint's own scope names only Decoration/Text as legacy entry points to converge, and Frame's Manage-Frames reorder/duplicate/delete identity is a materially bigger question; recorded as an open item in the new `docs/BUILDER_V3_CONVERGENCE_REPORT.md`. Verified via Playwright: clicking a Decoration glyph and "Add Text" both produce a real, correctly-attached Experience with zero orphan Scene Layers; the hosting-status banner and Host Here button/note both react correctly across hosted-here/hosted-elsewhere/never-hosted states; a full Museum Theme authoring pass using only the converged creation paths reaches a clean Validation and successful Scene/World Package Builds. Full regression across `goldenBuild.js` (30/30) and every prior Builder V3/V3.1/Working-View-Experience-Studio suite passes unchanged; zero console errors. No Engine V2/Scene Model/Runtime redesign; no second rendering implementation; no new Builder concepts.)

- Platform Integration Sprint ŌĆö Builder ŌåÆ Studio (a proof sprint, not a feature sprint, per its own explicit "the objective is not to build more, the objective is to prove the platform" instruction ŌĆö zero application code changed. Verified, end to end in one continuous Playwright session (one browser, two pages sharing one origin's `localStorage`, exactly how a real person would use two tabs ŌĆö no mocks, no manual file copying, no `storageState()` serialization shortcut), the complete real handoff the platform has always intended: a Theme authored in World Builder (real Overview identity, two genuinely-content-bearing uploaded images, a real Frame Experience named "Emerald Frame" with a distinct border colour, created through Scene ŌåÆ Place ŌåÆ "+ Add Experience") passes Validation with 0 errors/warnings, Builds into a real 21.84 KB `.vtheme`, and Publishes via "Publish to Official Themes" straight into the shared `localStorage['vihu.themeRegistry.imported.v1']` key ŌĆö the same key, same file, same origin Studio's own boot sequence already reads (`js/themeRegistry.js`'s `_loadImported()`), a mechanism implemented and documented in a much earlier sprint and now exercised for real rather than only asserted from code inspection.
